TAKE NOTE: The introduction is the EXACT same as every introduction for every
guide I've written. It's literally a copy/paste up to the Version History
section. So, if you've read another one of my walkthroughs, you can skip these
first sections should you so desire.

That being said, be forewarned: There is no censorship here. The following
guide is liable to contain mild swearing, crassness, unapologeticness, and bad
jokes. You have been warned.

If everything you see is not aligning correctly, try widening your window.
Could be you've got your window too narrow and it's shortening the margins.

Make sure you're viewing this guide in a fixed-width font. In order for the art
to work, it must be viewed in one of the following:

    * Courier New     <--   BEST (What I use)
    * Lucida Console  <--   GOOD
    * Consolas        <--   MEH
    * Courier         <--   OLD
    * Fixedsys        <--   WHY

This whole guide fits within the exact width of 79 characters. If you are not
sure whether or not you are using a fixed-width font, use the test below:

                      IIIIIIIIIIIIIII
                      WWWWWWWWWWWWWWW

If the row of I's and row of W's are perfectly aligned, then you are using a
fixed-width font. If absolutely all else fails, try to copy and paste the guide
into a text editor (like Notepad).

 /\  /\                             [NAVGD]                             /\  /\

Stuck on a particular part? Want to pick up where you left off? All that
scrolling can be such a pain!

Infommercialing aside, I've attempted to make navigating this guide as
enjoyable as doing something you don't want to do can be. You'll notice that
beside each item in the Table of Contents is a small code in brackets...
something like: [POOP]. You'll also eventually notice that the same code is
found at the corresponding section's heading. So, if you need to get to a
specific section, hit "CTRL"/"CMD" + "F" and type in the code WITH the
brackets. There's bound to be only 2-3 occurrences of each tag, so the find
function should take you straight to the section you are looking for.

If you printed this guide out... Well, you're shit ass out, you gotta flip
through it all. Sorry.

Also, the (at) in the address up there is just another method of mine to try to
avoid as much SPAMing as possible. This ensures that whoever emails me is
pretty much smart enough to figure out that it's the at sign emails use. Or
that I just told you. Either way, it helps to make sure most of my emails come
from humans, and that's great.

Additionally, please only email me if you have a serious question. I wrote this
guide to essentially answer all questions. If you ask me a question that I have
already answered here in some form, chances are I will simply defer you back to
this guide (although if I'm feeling nice and I usually am, then I'll mention
the specific section that you can find your answer in). Still, I encourage you
to look for the answer here before emailing as that will help cut down on the
amount of emails that we get.

If I get a bunch of repeat offenders (i.e. the same question asked by 5+
people) then I will put it in the FAQs section. If it does exist, then check
there to see if your question has already been asked repeatedly. If, after
you've exhausted all these options, your question remains unanswered, then
feel free to email me.

In addition, I won't give out my personal gamertag unless I personally know
you. Although, you'll probably find it out if you join the discord, in
which case: Friend me if you want, don't if you don't. But I reserve the right

is a right that I will usually exercise. Nothing against you, I just don't like
randos.

The Mobomu gamertag is just that: Mobomu. Same rules apply here as with my

Happy gaming.

Hi! Hercly Derkles here for Zelda Classic on PC, the most convenient way to
play The Legend of Zelda on your PC guaranteed! Seriously though, Zelda Classic
is awesome. If you would like to play The Legend of Zelda for free on your PC
at home, make your way to the following link:

                       http://www.zeldaclassic.com

There you will find all you need to install Zelda Classic on your PC and you'll
be off to the races. Now, this is NOT an emulator or anything like that, it is
an actual PC port/remake of the game. And to that end, it's even better than
the original. Because of its status as a full PC build, it is ever expandable,
has more quests than the original (and more will continue to come), and it has
enhanced graphics (think if Legend of Zelda came out on the SNES, so basically
just more vibrant).

So, yeah. I highly recommend Zelda Classic for some good ol' fashioned NES fun,
but better. The current version as of my writing this guide is Version 2.53.0.

You can download new quests made by fans from their website. I've included
links to the quest directory as well as my two favorite fan-made items. To play
them, just download the zip file, unzip it, and put the .qst file in the Zelda
Classic directory wherever you have it. Then select it from the Quest Options
menu in Zelda Classic.

      Quest Directories: 
      https://www.zeldaclassic.com/resource-listing/?filter_1=Quest
      https://wwww.purezc.net/index.php?page=quests

+--------------------------+
|--= ZELDA CLASSIC FAQS =--|
+--------------------------+

Q: How can I cheat in Zelda Classic?

A: Cheats are only enabled in certain quests. As an example, you cannot use
cheats in the First Quest on Zelda Classic.


Q: How do I get the custom quests?

A: From the character selection screen, select your character and press A (or
whatever you've keymapped A to be). This will take you to the Quest Options
menu. From there, you can press A to load a custom quest which will give you a
browse option to look for .qst files (only if you have not started playing on
this save).


Q: How do I make my own quests?

A: It's not the easiest thing in the world, but should you desire to make your
own Legend of Zelda quest, you can do so with the zquest.exe program in the
Zelda Classic director wherever you installed it. It's not a particularly
intuitive program and has little for documentation. There was once a good
online tutorial but it seems they've stopped paying the hosting fees. Perhaps
we'll make a video for it one day.


Q: I don't have the zquest.exe file, help!

A: Stop shouting. You probably either missed it or downloaded and earlier
version of Zelda Classic where it wasn't available yet. Make sure you have the
latest version and it should be there.

Now then: how about we move on to the content you actually came here for, shall
we?... The Legend of Zelda. The game that started it all. Zelda is a franchise
that has touched many people across many generations, and I consider it a
privilege to have experienced this franchise as I grew up. The first game was
revolutionary for its time and Zelda hasn't slowed down since. It's in my
Top 3 Favorite Gaming Franchises of All-Time list, usually around 1 or 2,
trading with Halo depending on my mood.
 
So, let's get this show on the road.

This section covers the controls of the game and how to make Link do the things
you need him to do in order to survive. And yes, I'm aware the controller in
the header is clearly an N64 Controller. That's because I like N64 and grew up
playing it. For Nintendo guides, it will always be an N64 controller. Deal with
it.

                             +--------------------+
                             |--= NES CONTROLS =--|
                             +--------------------+

                                        |
                       ________________/ \_______________
                      |           |_________|            |
                      |            _________             |
                      |     _     |_________|   NINTENDO |
                      |   _| |_     __   __   ,--,  ,--, |
                      |  |_ o _|   |__| |__|  |  |  |  | |
                      |    |_|     __\____\_  '--'  '--' |
                      |_____\_____|___\____\|_____\_____\|
                             \         \    \      \     \
                            D-Pad   Select  Start   B     A

Directional Pad (D-Pad): This is your walk controls. Use the directional pad
to guide Link around the map. Up, down, left, and right are the only four
directions you can really go. It also navigates the menus.

A Button: Your friendly neighborhood sword button. A controls your sword. It's
also how you select items in the menus.

B Button: If you have special items equipped on Link, you use them with B.

Start Button: Brings up the in-game menu.

Select Button: Pauses the game.

                             +--------------------+
                             |--= GBA CONTROLS =--|
                             +--------------------+

                    ______ .------------------------. ______
                   /_____.'                          '._____\
                  /            __________________         _  \
                 |    _       |                  |   _   / \  |
                 |  _| |_     |                  |  / \  \_/  |
                 | |_   _|    |                  |  \_/     \_|__ A
         D-Pad __|_/ |_|      |                  |     \______|__ B
                 |            |                  |            |
                 |    Start o |__________________|            |
                 '-. Select o                               .-'
                    '-.                                  .-'
                       '--------------------------------'

Directional Pad (D-Pad): This is your walk controls. Use the directional pad
to guide Link around the map. Up, down, left, and right are the only four
directions you can really go. It also navigates the menus.

A Button: Your friendly neighborhood sword button. A controls your sword. It's
also how you select items in the menus.

B Button: If you have special items equipped on Link, you use them with B.

Start Button: Brings up the in-game menu.

Select Button: Pauses the game.

                           +-----------------------+
                           |--= SWITCH CONTROLS =--|
                           +-----------------------+

                        ZL__                       __ZR
                            \   _L_         _R_   /
                             \.----'._____.'----./
                            .'    - |     | +    '.
                            | .--. \_Minus| / O   |
                            | |  |  |     |/ O O  |
                Left Stick__|/'--'  |Plus_/   O \_|__ A,B,X,Y
                            |       |     |  .--. |
                            |   O   |     |  |  | | 
                            |  O O  |     |  '--'\|__Right Stick
                 D-Buttons__|_/ O _ |     | _     |
                            '.   |_||     ||_|   .'
                              '.____|_____|____.'

Directional Buttons (D-Buttons): This is your walk controls. Use the
directional pad to guide Link around the map. Up, down, left, and right are the
only four directions you can really go. It also navigates the menus.

Left Stick: Can also be used to walk.

A Button: Your friendly neighborhood sword button. A controls your sword. It's
also how you select items in the menus.

B Button: If you have special items equipped on Link, you use them with B.

Plus Button: Acts as the start button. Used to select everything, also brings
up the in-game menu.

Minus Button: Acts as the select button. Navigates the menu, also pauses the
game.

ZL + ZR: Suspend Menu. Where you can create a new Suspend save, load an old
Suspend save, rewind what you've done, reset the game, or close it and return
to the NES catalog.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And that's all for the game's controls. The game was also ported to several
other Nintendo consoles, but the controls directly mirror one of the three
above so you should be able to figure it out from there. It's a very simple
game.

Here I'll cover the game basics, which is pretty much anything that I think may
be handy to know before we get started on the actual walkthrough.

   /\=====================================================================/\
  /__\---------------------={  M E C H A N I C S  }=---------------------/__\
 /\  /\                             [MECHS]                             /\  /\
/__\/__\===============================================================/__\/__\

Considering that at the time of my writing this The Legend of Zelda is 33 years
old, it's a very simple game by today's standards. As such, the mechanics are
simple, sweet, and intuitive. You hack and slash your way through enemies, grab
items you need, and complete Labyrinths until you have what it takes to fight
the big bad.

There are eight Labyrinths (try to do them in order if you're starting fresh
and using this guide) plus the final boss. Your view is consistently top-down
and the map is split into square areas that you can move between (more on this
further on). And that's pretty much it. Now that you know what's what, navigate
this world and its Labyrinths and rescue Princess Zelda!

   /\=====================================================================/\
  /__\--------------------={  C H A R A C T E R S  }=--------------------/__\
 /\  /\                             [CRCTR]                             /\  /\
/__\/__\===============================================================/__\/__\

With time the Legend of Zelda character roster will grow. But since this is the
first game, there are only five characters that we'll be encountering
throughout the game.

+------------+
|--= Link =--|
+------------+

Link is you, the main character, the Hero with a capital H. He's the
protagonist of every Zelda game, the one who people often call Zelda because
they're confused and perhaps a little lost as well, but his name's not Zelda
damn it, it's Link. In this game, Link is young, as he is in a fair amount of
the other series games, and he is only equipped with a wooden sword and shield
to start with. You ever used a wooden sword before? They're not very effective.
But Link is in possession of something more powerful than a measly sword:
courage, and the drive to save humanity.

+-------------+
|--= Ganon =--|
+-------------+

Ganon is the big bad bitch in this game (and really all of the Zelda games).
Later he is called Ganondorf (and the name Ganon is reserved for his monster
form). Here, Ganon takes control of the Triforce of Power and attempts to
control the entire world. Thankfully, someone like Link is around to give him
a swift kick to the plums instead.

+----------------------+
|--= Princess Zelda =--|
+----------------------+

The namesake of the entire franchise (for reasons, I guess). All this confusion
with Link/Zelda could have been avoided if they'd name the franchise after Link
instead of Zelda, though "The Legend of Link" doesn't sound as good. But "The
Adventure of Link" sounds pretty good and we'll get to that game after this
one. In The Legend of Zelda, Princess Zelda sends out her faithful companion/
guardian Impa to find a hero who can defeat Ganon. Unfortunately, Zelda is 
kidnapped by Ganon shortly afterwards and Link must save her as well!

+------------+
|--= Impa =--|
+------------+

Impa is technically not in the game, but she plays a pivotal role in the story
leading up to the start of the game. Impa is sent out by Zelda to find a hero
to fight Ganon. She finds Link just in time for him to defeat Ganon's henchmen
and embark on this epic quest to take down Ganon!

+---------------+
|--= Old Man =--|
+---------------+

The Old Man appears all throughout this game. There's no verifiable proof to
determine if he is one person or many, but we'll just assume he's one person
and he's here to help. He gives you the wooden Sword at the start of the game
and appears in each Labyrinth to give you hints if you can find him. And if you
whack him with your sword, his statues will shoot fireballs at you, so don't do
that. Or do, up to you.


 ,----------.=====================================================,----------.
/\\ ~~~~~    \   IV         S E C T I O N   F O U R         IV   / ~~~~~    //\
\/_\ ~~~~~~~~ \-------------------------------------------------/ ~~~~~~~~ /_\/
   | ~~~~~~~~ |         T H E   S T O R Y   S O   F A R         | ~~~~~~~~ |

 / ~~~~~~~~ /                                                     \ ~~~~~~~~ \
/ ~~~~~~~~ /                        [STORY]                        \ ~~~~~~~~ \
/\¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯\---------------------------------------------------/¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯/\
\/           /                  www.mobomu.com                   \           \/
 '----------'====================================================='----------'

A LONG, LONG TIME AGO THE WORLD WAS IN AN AGE OF CHAOS.

In the midst of this chaos, in a little kingdom in the land of Hyrule, a legend 
was being handed down from generation to generation, the legend of the 
"Triforce"; golden triangles possessing mystical powers. One day, an evil army 
attacked this peaceful little kingdom and stole the Triforce of Power. This 
army was led by Ganon, the powerful Prince of Darkness who sought to plunge the 
World into fear and darkness under his rule. Fearing his wicked rule, Zelda, 
the princess of this kingdom, split up the Triforce of Wisdom into eight 
fragments and hid them throughout the realm to save the last remaining Triforce 
from the clutches of the evil Ganon. At the same time, she commanded her most 
trustworthy nursemaid, Impa, to secretly escape into the land and go find a man 
with enough courage to destroy the evil Ganon. Upon hearing this, Ganon grew 
angry, imprisoned the princess, and sent out a party in search of Impa.

Braving forests and mountains, Impa fled for her life from her pursuers. As she 
reached the very limit of her energy she found herself surrounded by Ganon's 
evil henchmen. Cornered! What could she do? ... But wait! All was not lost. A 
young lad appeared. He skillfully drove off Ganon's henchmen, and saved Impa 
from a fate worse than death.

His name was Link. During his travels he had come across Impa and Ganon's 
henchmen. Impa told Link the whole story of the princess Zelda and the evil 
Ganon. Burning with a sense of justice, Link resolved to save Zelda, but Ganon 
was a powerful opponent. He held the Triforce of power. And so, in order to 
fight off Ganon, Link had to bring the scattered eight fragments of the 
Triforce of Wisdom together to rebuild the mystical triangle. If he couldn't do 
this, there would be no chance Link could fight his way into Death Mountain 
where Ganon lived.

Can Link really destroy Ganon and save Princess Zelda? 

Only your skill can answer that question. Good luck. Use the Triforce wisely.

(above story copyrighted to Nintendo, (c) 1986)

This walkthrough was written based on my approximately 4th playthrough. I'm
now playing on the Nintendo Switch Online version of the game and it's quite
nice, I highly recommend it if you have a Switch, which if you're reading this
guide you probably do.

The walkthrough will take you through the game and also help you to get every
item, heart container, and secret that there is in the game. This section is
dedicated to the First Quest Playthrough and the Second Quest playthrough will
follow.

**NOTE**: I refer directly to the maps I've created for this walkthrough
constantly. It's the only effective way to write a walkthrough for this game in
my opinion. The maps operate on a grid coordinate system and are fairly
straight-forward. However, I would recommend you print out the MAP section
further down to have as a quick reference, or at least open this guide in
another tab and keep it on the map section. It'll make your life easier.

**ANOTHER NOTE**: Things that I think are important for you to see or pickup
will be in all CAPS and surrounded by a hyphequal sign (I made that up),
-=LIKE THIS=-, so that they stand out to you as you're reading.

                 +------------------------------------------+
                 |--= HOW TO GET TO EACH SECTION QUICKLY =--|
                 +------------------------------------------+
                 | --= CTRL/CMD + F                         |
                 |                                          |
                 | --= Copy & Paste the Commands:           |
                 |              [EXAMPLE]                   |
                 |                                          |
                 | --= Click "Find" until you get to the    |
                 |     right section                        |
                 +------------------------------------------+

QUICK TIPS:

1. When you die in the Overworld, you'll start back at the original screen in
the game, coordinate H8. If you die in a Labyrinth, you'll start at the
beginning of that Labyrinth.

2. Saving is love; Saving is life. Save often. If you're playing on an NES,
make sure to hold down the reset button to shut off so you don't lose your save
data.

3. Watch your health always. If you hear the "beep, beep", best be getting some
hearts or you're gonna die.

4. Rupees. Grab every rupee you see no matter what. Die for the rupees (don't
though). You want to be stockpiling your rupees constantly because you need
them constantly.

5. Lastly, this game has been around for 30+ years and different people play it
differently. There are many strategies to conquering The Legend of Zelda and
we're going to do this in a more casual, the way it was meant to be played
style. So, we're not going to be doing a get every item for Labyrinth One
strategy, nor will we be heading directly to Labyrinth One.

The strategy outlined in this walkthrough is, in my opinion, the ideal strategy
for the best playing experience to be garnered from this game. I hope you enjoy
The Legend of Zelda and let's dig in:

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S T A R T I N G   O U T                                           [101-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You will start the game on Coordinate H8. Thankfully, there are no enemies
because you are unarmed! Well, you have a shield. But it's a shitty Wooden
Shield. So, we need to do some prepping.

Head forward to the cave in this coordinate and you'll find an Old Man waiting
inside.

            "I T ' S   D A N G E R O U S   T O   G O   A L O N E!
                            T A K E    T H I S."

The Old Man will give you a -=WOODEN SWORD=-. It's super ineffective! Gee,
thanks, Old Man. Take the sword from the Old Man and exit the Cave. Don't worry
about the sword, we'll get a better one in no time. Now, how to use your
shield: It will block incoming objects from whatever direction so long as you
AREN'T swinging your sword while it hits you. No sword swing = shield up.
That's how it works.

It's from this point that most players choose to go straight to the first
dungeon, but the way I see it: that's just making life more difficult than it
has to be. In a few minutes, we can get some bombs, the blue candle, some heart
containers, a better sword and shield, potions, and the blue ring. Why wouldn't
you do that before jumping into a dungeon, right?

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   B O M B S ,   B O M B S ,   B O M B S                             [101-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proceed west from the start to H7 where you'll be confronted by four Tektites.
Kill them from afar with your sword beams (as long as you have full health,
you'll be shooting nice and shiny sword lasers from far away). Take whatever
they drop for you and proceed north to G7. Kill the four Red Octoroks and take
your goodies. Enter the cave here to enter World Shop 1.

And look at that. They have the -=BLUE CANDLE=- in stock. And for only 60
rupees, what a steal! Okay, that may seem steep now, but it's really not that
bad for what you're getting. So, we need to save up 60 rupees. That shouldn't
be too hard.

Return to H8, the starting point, and now we're going to head east until we
can't go east anymore, through H9, H10, H11, H12, H13, H14, H15, and lastly
H16. Kill everything you can along the way. H9 has a squad of Red Octoroks for
you to take care of H10 and H11 have Tektites ready and waiting to perish by
your blade. H12 you'll be attacked by Leevers as soon as you step into the area
and a Zola will fire at you from the water. H13 continues along the beach with
more Leevers as that pesky Zola keeps shooting at you. H14 has a pack of Blue
Octoroks and H15 has (mercifully) Red Octoroks. When you finally reach H16
there will be a single Blue Octorok for you to kill before continuing north to
G16.

Take care of the mixed Red and Blue Octoroks here and head into the cave for
World Shop 2. Here you can buy -=BOMBS=- for 20 rupees if you haven't had any
drop for you yet (it's pretty rare that I don't get bombs to drop for me on the
way, but on the off chance that you don't, the shop is a convenient failsafe).
Drop the 20 rupees if you need to and then exit the shop.

Now just head back and forth between here and H8 and keep killing the enemies
until you have 60 rupees (it shouldn't take long at all, I had 85 rupees after
two passes). (Note: the enemies do respawn, it just takes a little bit. By the
time you've reached the end of the loop, they should be spawning where you came
from.) Alternatively, you can try your luck with the Gambling Game. Head west
one from the origin to H7. Here you want to bomb the north wall 5 tiles to the
left of the north path. Use the map for help.

            _______________________     ___
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|   |#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|G|#|#|#|#|.'   |#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯      |#|#|
                           |#|  _      '.|#|     KEY:
                _     _     _  |#|       '-.
               |#|   |#|   |#|                    G  - Gambling Den
                ¯     ¯     ¯  |#|       .-'      #  - Rock
                           |#|  ¯      .'|#|
            ___________________________|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Inside the cave you've made, the Old Man will present you with three options,
each at -10 rupees. The way the game works is you pick one of the options. Two
of the three subtract rupees while one adds them. If you pick the additive one,
you make a quick buck. Usually, one of the subtractive ones is more damaging
than the other. After you pick, the options will change to show you what they
were. You then have to leave and reenter the cave to reset it. If you run out
of rupees, kill some enemies around here to get more OR save your game before
entering and reset every time you run out.

However you chose to get rupees, return to the shop at coordinate G7 once you
have 60 and purchase the Blue Candle. Hooray! A few minutes and we already have
bombs and the Blue Candle.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   B O Y   W H O   H A D   H E A R T S                       [101-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we've got bombs and a Blue Candle, it's time we grabbed some extra
Heart Containers. After all that combat, I'm sure you're just itching to no
longer be restricted by your three heart limitations. It's okay, me too.

To get Heart Container 1, return to the origin coordinate (H8). Head east all
the way through to H12 (the first area with water). Kill all the Leevers again
so that there's some peace and quiet (except for that bastard Zola that's still
taking shots from the water like a chump). Equip your bombs and bomb the wall
-=TWO TILES TO THE LEFT OF THE NORTH PATHWAY=- to reveal a hidden cave. Use the
map for help.

            _____________________       ___
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|     |#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|H|#|     |#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|.'¯¯¯   ¯       ¯¯¯
           |#|#|#|#|#|.'                          KEY:
           |#|.'.|#|.'
            ¯¯   ¯¯¯       ________________       H  - Heart Container
            --.------.    / ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|      #  - Rock
           |#|#|#|#|#|'. | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |      ~  - Water
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|'|~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#| ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Enter the cave to find our good friend the Old Man. You know, the one that gave
you this piece of crap sword. Yep, the very same (we think). He'll give you a
choice between a bottle of red potion and a -=HEART CONTAINER=-. Don't you dare
pick the potion. Grab the Heart Container and return to the Overworld once
more.

From here head North to G12, west to G9, north to E9, and then west to E8.
Equip your Blue Candle and count -=FIVE BUSHES=- from the right and use the
Blue Candle on the fifth bush to reveal a stair way. Use the map to help you.

            _______________________________
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|     KEY:
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯       H  - Heart Container
            _____________________   _______       %  - Bush
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|H|%|%|%|%|      ~  - Water
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|

            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Head down it to meet our Old Man for the second time. I swear to God, if you
pick the potion, we'll have words. Grab your second -=HEART CONTAINER=- and
return to the Overworld. 

From here head east to E9, then north to C9. Beeline east ignoring the Peahats
and continue east to C13. Kill the four Tektites here and then bomb the -=LOWER
RIGHT SIDE OF THE CENTRAL ROCK FORMATION=- to reveal another cave. Use the map
to help you.

            _____   _______________________
           |#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯   ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|#|#|#|#|
                       .'|#|#|'.   |#|#|#|#|     KEY:
                     .'|#|#|#|#|'. '.|#|#|#|
                     |#|#|#|#|#|#|   ¯¯¯¯¯¯       H  - Heart Container
                     '.|#|#|#|H|.'                #  - Rock 
                       ¯¯¯¯¯¯                    |-| - Stairs
            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯


Enter to find the same Old Man and the same choice. I've told you time and
again! Don't take the potion! Grab your third -=HEART CONTATINER=- from the Old
Man. And now you have six hearts. That means we're worthy enough to wield the
White Sword.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A   L E T T E R                                                   [101-4]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before we grab the White Sword, it's easier if we make a quick detour now to
grab the Letter. Pop over east once more to C14. Kill the Octoroks if you wish
and then head north along the pathway (not the stairs) to B14. Ignore the
Peahats and the stairs here and head east once more to B15. The stairs HERE are
the ones you need to use, and they will lead you up to A15 where there is a
another cave entrance.

Enter the hole and don't pay the troll toll. Inside will be the Old Man again
and he will tell you to "Show this to the Old Woman." So, grab the -=LETTER=-
and marvel at the Old Man's teleporting abilities before returning once more
to the Overworld. That's all we have to do for this quest right this second.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S O M E   R E A L   G E A R                                       [101-5]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Return to C13 and head west to C9 and kill all the Leevers on the way. When you
get to C9 head west one more to C8 and then north to B8, ignoring the Peahats
as you go. You now find yourself in the Death Mountain region. Beware of
falling rock.

Move quickly, avoiding the rocks, and head east to B11 (the screen with all the
Tektites and the blue staircase leading up Death Mountain). Avoid the Tektites
(or kill them) and head up the staircase to A11. Here there's a pond in the
center with a Zola in it and a Blue Lynel patrolling the area. Kill or avoid
the Lynel (probably avoid for now) and get into the cave in the upper left
corner of the area. You'll find the Old Man inside once more but this time with
the -=WHITE SWORD=-.

           "M A S T E R   U S I N G   I T   A N D   Y O U   C A N
                            H A V E   T H I S."

Grab the White Sword and rejoice for your sword no longer sucks. This puppy can
one shot most of the little turds you've been hacking away at until now. Now
that we have a better sword, we need a better shield. And my axe!

Now we could head to the shop at G16 and pick one up for 130 rupees, but what
if I told you... that we can get one for 90 rupees? To do so, you need to
backtrack all the way to the origin point (H8). From the origin, head west one,
north one, west one, north one, and then east one to F7. I killed everything on
the way in an attempt to maximize my rupee earnings and made a whopping one
rupee the whole way. So, you decide on that one. However, you do need to make
sure you have 90 rupees when you get to F7, so do that (either by the farming
loop or the gambling cave).

Once you reach F7, head north one more time to E7. Use the Blue Candle on the
-=BUSH IN THE CORNER=- where the path bends to reveal a staircase.  Use the map
for help.

            _______________________________
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|      KEY:
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~_________________|
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|                        S  - Shop 3
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |    _____________       %  - Bush
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|    S|%|%|%|%|%|%|      ~  - Water
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯


Head down the staircase to find a shop with the Magical Shield for sale at a
price of 90 rupees. Drop your ka-ching on the shield and return to the
Overworld.

Right, so we've got our sword and our shield now. Just a few things left on our
pre-flight checklist here.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   P O S T M A N   L I N K                                           [101-6]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we have six hearts, the White Sword, and the Magic Shield, things are
going to be considerably easier. But we can still bump this cake walk up a
notch. To end the Letter quest and unlock the Potion Shops, we need to get to
G5. And while we're over there, we can also shoot up to D5 and grab the Blue
Ring, which halves Link's incoming damage.

There's just one catch: the Blue Ring costs 250 rupees. But the good news is
that we don't have to run the rupee farm loop or gamble like addicts until we
have 250 rupees, there are better ways to make rupees now. You'll notice on the
map that there are a series of rupee gifts hidden throughout Hyrule. You may be
saying, "Hey WTF, Herc? Why didn't we use those before?" Well, cause we needed
them for now. So, we're gonna stop off and grab one of these rupee gifts on the
way to deliver the letter.

We need to get to G12 first, so from E7: head east two, south two, and east
three to G12. Kill the handful of Moblins and Octoroks here and then get your
Blue Candle ready. Burn the -=BOTTOM BUSH=- in the stack of three on the right.
Use the map for help.

            _   _       _   _   ___   _____
           |%| |%|     |%| |%| |%|%| |%|%|%|
           |%| |%|     |%| |%| |%|%| |%|%|%|
            ¯   ¯       ¯   ¯   ¯¯¯   ¯|%|%|
                _       _   _  |%|      ¯|%|     KEY:
               |%|     |%| |%|  _         ¯ 
                            _  |%|                R  - 100 Rupees
               |%|     |%|  R|            _       %  - Bush
                ¯       ¯   ¯  |%|      _|%|
            _________________          |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|         |%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯           ¯¯¯

Head down the stairs you've unearthed and grab the 100 rupees. Now then, let's
deliver that letter. Head west all the way to G5.

Kill the Octoroks here and then head into the cave. Equip the Letter the Old
Man gave you earlier and give it to the Old Woman inside. You have now unlocked
the ability to buy Potions at a Potion Shop. The Blue Potion costs 40 rupees
and the Red Potion costs 68 rupees. The difference is you can use a Red Potion
twice, so always buy the Red Potions. If you buy a potion right now, you'll
need to make that money back for the Blue Ring.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   O N E   R I N G                                           [101-7]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now there's one more 100-rupee gift we can get here to help us afford the Blue
Ring. IMPORTANT NOTE: You can either get these 100 rupees now or save it for
just before the Demon Labyrinth (Level 7) where you'll need 100 rupees for a
Bomb Upgrade. Your choice between taking the convenience now or later. If you
plan to skip out on the 100-rupee gift now, jump to the paragraph after the
map.

Head east into the Lost Woods (characterized by brown bushes instead of green)
two screens to G3 and kill the Moblins here. Then burn the -=TOPMOST BUSH=-
in the single column that bisects the screen here and grab the 100 rupees from
inside. Use the map for help.

            _________     ___           ___
           |%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|    ¯ R|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|     |%|          ¯¯¯      KEY:
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯      |%|
                           |%|                    R  - 100 Rupees
            ___________    |%|_________           %  - Bush
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|___
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Now that have 250 rupees, we're trying to get to coordinate D5. So, from the
Potion Shop at G5 just head north three screens and you're there. You should be
in an area with six Armos statues in it. Touch the -=TOP-MIDDLE=- Armos and it
will begin to move around, revealing a staircase where it once stood. Use the
map for help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|.'¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|#|#|
           |#|  _   _   _              '.|#|     KEY:
           |#| |A|  S| |A|               |#|
           |#|      ¯          __________|#|      S  - Shop 4
           |#| |A| |A| |A|    /~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |      A  - Armos
           |#|  ¯   ¯   ¯    |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|      #  - Rock
           |#|'.___________  | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |      ~  - Water
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#| |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#| | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Descend the staircase to find World Shop 4. Here you can purchase the Blue Ring
from the merchant for the low, low price of 250 rupees. Fork over all your hard
earned rupees and get the Blue Ring. Now that you've got your fancy blue
(white, though) tunic, we're ready for the first Labyrinth.

Return south three screens to G5, then east to G9, and then north to D9. Cross
the bridge to D8 where you'll find the entrance to the Eagle Labyrinth.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 2                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE EAGLE              ___________________/   [CH102]      /\  /\

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   F L Y   L I K E   A N   E A G L E                                 [102-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- F3 - Immediately upon entering you're faced with three doors. The door
leading north is locked, so head right to F4 first.

-- F4 - You'll find yourself faced with a group of five Stalfos. Eliminate them
all and one will drop a -=KEY=-. Take the key then return to F3.

-- F3 - Head left now to F2.

-- F2 - Kill the three Keese flying around the room and a second -=KEY=- will
appear. Grab it and return to F3 again.

-- F3 - Now we can head further into the Labyrinth. Use one of your keys on the
north door and head through.

-- E3 - There will be three Stalfos in here. Dispatch them easily enough and
proceed north again to D3.

-- D3 - Another big group of Stalfos await you in this room. Kill them all and
another -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the new key and head right to D4.

-- D4 - Kill all of the Keese in this room and grab the nice and shiny
-=COMPASS=- sitting on the floor. Return back to D3.

-- D3 - Head across and left to D2.

-- D2 - As you enter this room, the door will barricade behind you. There are a
lot of Keese in here so kill them quickly and pick up whatever they drop. Once
all are dead, the door to D3 will reopen. Ignore it for now and go north
through the locked door, using one of your keys.

-- C2 - Kill the three Gels in here to give yourself some breathing room.
You'll notice that once the Gels are dead, the barricade to your left doesn't
open. Hmm. There's a -=SINGULAR BLOCK=- in the middle of the room. Push it to
the right and the barricade will open. Head through the new door.

-- C1 - There will be an Old Man here and he'll give you a hint.

             "E A S T M O S T   P E N N I N S U L A   I S   T H E
                                S E C R E T ."

You'll note that they misspelled "peninsula" (in the Switch version this is
fixed and spelled properly). That's all from the Old Man so head back to C2.

-- C2 - Head across and to the right to C3.

-- C3 - Kill all of the Gels in here and then grab the -=MAP=-. Not that you
really needed it since I've provided you with one at the start. Still, it's
nice to have a quick reference of your whereabouts. Once you have the map,
head north through the open door.

-- B3 - You will find yourself in a water-filled room with a single pathway
tracing around it. There are three Stalfos on the pathway. Kill them all and
grab the -=KEY=- that one of them drops. Continue north through the locked
door.

-- A3 - There are three Goriyas here throwing their boomerangs all willy-nilly.
Approach them carefully and take them out and a -=KEY=- will appear. Take the
key and continue through the locked door to your left.

-- A2 - Watch out for the Traps as soon as you enter! You'll notice immediately
in this room a staircase surrounded by blocks. You need to push the -=LEFTMOST
BLOCK=- up to access the staircase.

                      _
                    _|_|_           KEY:
                  _|_| |_|_
                 |P|  S  | |        P - Push Block
                  ¯|¯| |¯|¯         S - Stairs
                    ¯|¯|¯
                      ¯

Once you've gained access to the stairs, head down them to a basement room.
Kill off the four Keese in here and then grab the -=BOW=- from the platform on
the right. Once you have the Bow, return up the stairs to A2 and back track to
C3.

-- C3 - Head through the locked door to the right now, using your last key for
now.

-- C4 - In this next room are three more Goriyas flinging their boomerangs
every which way. Kill them and a -=BOOMERANG=- of your very own will appear at
the top of the room. Pick it up and continue right to C5.

-- C5 - Watch out for the Wall Masters in here! You'll need to grab the -=KEY=-
in this room while avoiding the Wall Masters and if they grab you, they'll take
you all the way back to the beginning of the Labyrinth. Once you have the key,
hurry north through the locked door.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
     H E       R   B A L L ?                                         [102-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the Dragondome. Get it? Cause Aquamentus is a dragon. Now I hope
you're ready for a fight cause... well, Aquamentus is pretty easy. So, let's
kick some dragon ass.
    _____________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: A Q U A M E N T U S   \_________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A type of dragon that some call a unicorn.   | Received:              |
  |  As well as having lots of attack power, it's  |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  a fearful opponent. It emits beams."          |  -- Triforce Piece 1   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Shoots a burst of three fireballs at you. Each fireball does a       |
  |    half heart of damage with the Blue Ring equipped                     |
  |  - That's it.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full heart containers going into the fight, just sit in  |
  |    the back and shoot sword beams at him. He'll die after a few hits.   |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The other strategy is to wait for him to fire a volley of fireballs, |
  |    dodge the projectiles, and then run up close and slash him. In my    |
  |    opinion, this is quicker and easier than shooting sword beams.       |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have the White Sword (which you should), he'll die after      |
  |    three hits.                                                          |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Beyond shooting fireballs, he barely even moves. He's a very         |
  |    stationary boss, so use that to your advantage when going in for     |
  |    the kill.                                                            |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Aquamentus is a very easy boss (not surprising considering he's the    |
  |  first boss of the game. Shoot him with sword beams or wait for         |
  |  fireball volley and run up to slash him. You should be able to kill    |
  |  him without much fuss and get on to other things.                      |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Once Aquamentus has fallen, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- he leaves behind and
head through the door to the right. Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and
you'll get a nice little animation and be conveniently teleported to exiting
the Labyrinth and that's it. Eagle Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   O N W A R D   Y O U N G   W A R R I O R                           [102-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There's not too much to do besides heading straight for the Moon Labyrinth. I'd
suggest picking up a Red Potion if you don't have one just in case and then
we're off.

We need to navigate to coordinate D13. Back track to the origin (H8) and head
all the way east until you can't go east anymore (H16). Now head north one
screen and then west two screens. Follow the path north two screens and then
head west one screen. There will be five Octoroks here and a flight of stairs
leading north. Kill the Octoroks and take the stairs up to the entrance of the
Moon Labyrinth.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 3                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE MOON               ___________________/   [CH103]      /\  /\

                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P

                       +-------------------------------+
                       |--=           KEY           =--|
                       +-------------------------------+
                       |                               |
                       | E - Entrance                  |
                       | K - Key                       |
                       | M - Map                       |
                       | C - Compass                   |
                       | I - Item                      |
                       | B - Boss Fight                |
                       | T - Triforce Segment          |
                       | O - Old Man                   |
                       | # - Connected Stairs          |
                       | R - Rupee Room                |
                       | G - Hungry Goriya             |
                       | x - Locked Door               |
                       | + - Barricade Door            |
                       | ! - Bombable Wall             |
                       |                               |
                       +-------------------------------+

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   H E R E   C O M E S   T H E   M O O N                             [103-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H2 - Starting out, you have two choices: up or right. Head right into H3.

-- H3 - You'll be confronted by a pack of roaming Ropes. Take them all out
(careful, they move really fast) and a -=KEY=- will appear in the center of the
room. Grab the key and head up through the next door.

-- G3 - Kill the handful of Ropes here and head through the left door.

-- G2 - More Ropes. Kill them back, Guardian. Once they're all dead the door to
the left will open. Proceed through it.

-- G1 - Kill all the Ropes in here and grab the -=KEY=- they were guarding.
Once you have the key head back right all the way to G3.

-- G3 - Using one of your new keys, unlock the door to the right and head
through it.

-- G4 - Kill all of the Gels in here to get them out of your way and then grab
the -=COMPASS=- from the corner. Now equip your bombs and bomb the top wall
(from here on out: when I say to bomb a wall in a Labyrinth, I mean to bomb the
middle of that wall. It's always going to be the middle of the wall where a
door would be in Labyrinths) to create a passageway to F4. Head through it.

-- F4 - Take out the gels in here and then pick up the -=MAP=- in the center of
the room. Now bomb the top wall in here as well. Head through the new door.

-- E4 - E4 is a terrible, terrible place. There will be three Blue Goriyas in
the middle of the room throwing their boomerangs like mad and accompanying them
in the four corners of the room are four Stone Statues peppering you constantly
with fireballs. If you can make it out of here without taking damage, you're a
god. Kill the three Goriyas and the -=MAGICAL BOOMERANG=- will appear in the
center of the room. Grab it and leave immediately through the door on the left.

-- E3 - Upon entering this room, the door to the south will slam shut. Kill the
Ropes in here and pick up whatever they drop. When all of them are defeated,
the lower door will open and a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the key. Now, if you
want, you can head south to F3 and kill all the Goriyas in there for hearts if
you need them, but there are a lot so be careful (and this way you don't have
to unlock the door between F3 and F4). Once you're ready to proceed, head up
to D3.

-- D3 - Now we've got a desert room and extra special just for you: two
Moldorms. Slash the Moldorms to bits (they're easy) and once they're both
defeated, a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the key and then head to the right.

-- D4 - Watch out for the Traps! Kill the few Keese in here and then grab the
-=BOMBS=- from this room. If you were bombing the walls like I told you to,
then you need to replenish your supply. Now head back to D3 and then up to C3.

-- C3 - There's a ton of Ropes in here so dispatch them as quickly as you can.
Maybe you'll get lucky and one of them will drop a Stopwatch. Once they've all
been defeated the top door will open but before we head through there, proceed
to the right through the locked door.

-- C4 - Kill the five Gels in here and five rupees will appear in the middle of
the room. Pick that up and then head north to B4.

-- B4 - We've found the Old Man again and he'll once more give us a clue.

              "D O D O N G O   D I S L I K E S   S M O K E ."

This one is much less cryptic than the peninsula one. He's simply telling us a
mechanic for the upcoming boss fight. Say bye to the Old Man and head back down
then left to C3.

-- C3 - Now head north through the other door to B3.

-- B3 - This is the last room we'll hang out in before fighting the Dodongo.
It's also full of Goriyas. Use the blocks in the room to your advantage and
kill all of the Goriyas. Take whatever they drop and once you've killed them
all some more bombs will appear in the upper right corner of the room. Grab
them if you need them and then suck in your gut cause we got a boss to kill.
Head through the top door.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   M O R E   L I K E   D O D U N G O                                 [103-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And just like that we're already fighting the next boss. Now I hope you're
ready for a fight this time cause... well, Dodongo is also pretty easy. Let's
bomb his butt (literally).
    _______________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: D O D O N G O   \_______________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A giant rhinoceros. It hasn't got so much    | Received:              |
  |  attacking power, but it bounces off attacks   |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  with its thick hide"                          |  -- Triforce Piece 2   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Just like the description says, the Dodongo doesn't have much        |
  |    attacking power, in that it doesn't attack at all.                   |
  |  - He just walks around the room.                                       |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The Dodongo is impervious to everything in your arsenal except bombs |
  |    but you probably guessed that cause the Labyrinth gave you bombs     |
  |    twice and you were smart enough to figure out the Old Man's clue.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - As the Dodongo walks around the room, lay a bomb in its path. As it  |
  |    walks over the bomb, it will eat it and then the bomb will explode   |
  |    inside it. Do this twice and the Dodongo will perish.                |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If for whatever reason the Dodongo doesn't eat your bomb, the smoke  |
  |    will still stun it (this is what the Old Man was talking about) and  |
  |    you can run up and slash him to bits during that window.             |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Dodongo is probably the easiest boss in this game. Drop bombs in his   |
  |  path twice or stun him with smoke and hack away with your sword. This  |
  |  is an easy win so dispatch him and I'll see you on the other side.     |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Hey! You beat Dodongo! Good job. Pretty tough, right? Once he's dead grab the
-=HEART CONTAINER=- he leaves behind for you and head through the door to the
left. Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and you'll be teleported to the
Labyrinth entrance. Moon Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   J O U R N E Y   C O N T I N U E S                         [103-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There's not much to do after beating the Moon Labyrinth other than head to the
Manji Labyrinth, and by not much I mean nothing at all. The Manji Labyrinth
entrance is at coordinate H5, which is right next to the origin coordinate.
Unfortunately, it's not as simple as just heading west from the origin.

So, make your way back to H8 and then head west once, north once, west three
(grab a potion from the Old Lady if you need), and west once more into G4 and
the Lost Woods. Immediately head south one then east one to H5 where you will
find the entrance to the Manji Labyrinth. Enter if you dare.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 4                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE MANJI              ___________________/   [CH104]      /\  /\
/__\/__\ __________________________/           \______________________ /__\/__\

|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|

|  [104-3]  Continuing to Continue     - Make your way to Snake Labyrinth     |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   L E A V E   Y O U R   W O R L D   B E H I N D                     [104-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- F4 - Starting out there's only one possible way to go, so head left to F3.

-- F3 - There are several Zols in this room (just larger versions of Gels), but
they won't be an issue since we already have the White Sword. You'll also
notice a -=KEY=- in the middle of the room. Kill the Zols, making sure to grab
whatever they drop, and grab the key. Continue up to E3.

-- E3 - Another pack of Zols awaits you here, so dispatch them and they'll drop
another -=KEY=-. Grab the key and continue the only way you can go: up to D3.

-- D3 - There are three Darknuts here for you to face. You cannot damage them
from head-on thanks to their shields, so get behind them or beside them before
slashing. If you have full health, sword beams make landing shots on them a lot
easier. Bombs can also be useful. Once they're defeated, they'll drop some
-=BOMBS=- for you. Grab them if you want and then head left to D2.

-- D2 - Watch out for the Traps when you enter! You'll notice the -=COMPASS=-
in the middle of the room here and some Keese. Kill the Keese and then grab the
Compass. Use one of your keys on the door to the left and head into D1.

-- D1 - In here there will be six more Darknuts. Eliminate them however you
choose and once they're all dead, the door to the south will open. Head south
to E1.

-- E1 - Welcome to yet another room with a metric ton of Darknuts. Dispatch
them however you can. They tend to drop a lot of bombs, so I'd recommend using
bombs to clear a few of them out before switching to hack 'n' slashing the
rest. Grab what you can and then head down the stairs to the basement. In the
basement, head down the stairs killing the Keese as you go. Once the Keese are
taken care of, grab the -=RAFT=- from the platform to the right and then return
up the stairs. Once back on the main floor, head up twice to C1.

-- C1 - In here there will be two Zols, a few Keese, and three Bubbles. You
can't damage the Bubbles with your sword so tend to the other enemies then grab
the -=KEY=- from the center of the room and exit to the right.

-- C2 - Entering this room from the left restricts you to a narrow path through
the center of the room. Kill the Keese and a bomb drop will spawn in the path.
Grab the bombs if you need and then continue through the locked door to the
right.

-- C3 - Now we are in one of the centermost rooms for this Labyrinth, which
presents a lot of options for where to go next. First things first, kill the
three Zols in here and grab the -=KEY=- that spawns once they're dead. Now, we
can rule out going South since we've already been to D3. So, we've got up or to
the right. We're going to head up first, so use a key on the top door and head
through.

-- B3 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! There are two Zols in here to go
ahead and take them out. Now then, the door ahead is blocked, and we have two
blocks in here. Push the left block one more space to the left and the door
will open. Continue upward.

-- A3 - Here we'll encounter the Old Man once more with another hint for us.

         "D I D   Y O U   G E T   T H E   S W O R D   F R O M   T H E
                   O L D   M A N   O N   T O P   O F   T H E
                             W A T E R F A L L ?"

He's referring to the White Sword here and we've had that for quite some time.
Move on through the door to the left.

-- A2 - The door will promptly close behind you as you enter, and you'll be
trapped with a number of Keese. Kill them all and grab the -=KEY=- in this
room. Now then, backtrack to our central room: C3.

-- C3 - Now we're going to through the locked door to the right.

-- C4 - Watch out for the Traps as you enter! Kill the Zols in the center of
the room here and grab the -=MAP=-. Why they put the map so far in this
Labyrinth is beyond me, but we don't really need it anyway, so no big deal.
Now, we're about to face Manhandla. If you like, you can head down one to D4
and kill the enemies there for some rupees or a chance at some health. Whenever
you're read bomb the right wall here and step through to the boss's chamber.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A N   U N F O R T U N A T E   N A M E                             [104-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clap the chalk off your hands because we're breezing through this game. Now I
hope you're actually ready for a fight this time cause... well, Manhandla is
pretty easy too. Let's give him a slap.
    ___________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: M A N H A N D L A   \___________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A large man-eating flower with hands         | Received:              |
  |  sticking out in all four directions. It moves |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  faster as it loses hands. It's pretty mean.   |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |  So watch out!"                                |                        |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - It'll charge at you with flailing arms and give you a good whack.    |
  |  - It also shoots fireballs from every orifice, of which there are a    |
  |    good number.                                                         |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - There's one surefire way to kill the Manhandla with a single blow.   |
  |    You need to drop a bomb in its path in just the right way that it    |
  |    will explode when the Manhandla is centered on it. This will blow    |
  |    all of its limbs off in one fell swoop and that'll be that. You need |
  |    to be accurate with your bombs. It's much easier said than done.     |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The actual strategy here is to hack off its limbs with your sword    |
  |    (two hits per limb with the White Sword). It'll speed up as you      |
  |    delimb it until all of its arms have been cut off.                   |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Manhandla is a real slapper. Try to nail it with a bomb in dead center |
  |  to blow all its limbs off or hack away at the arms with your sword.    |
  |  It shouldn't give you too much trouble.                                |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
And just like that, another one bites the dust. Once he's dead grab the -=HEART
CONTAINER=- he leaves behind for you and head through the door to above. Grab
the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and you'll be teleported to the Labyrinth entrance.
Manji Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   C O N T I N U I N G   T O   C O N T I N U E                       [104-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Head back to the origin point (H8) by going west one, north one, east four,
south one. And you're back. This time we do actually have some small errands to
take care of before we jump on into the Snake Labyrinth.

From origin, head all the way east to H16. From H16 head north one screen to
G16. Head into the store here and drop some rupees on a bundle of arrows and
have your Bow equipped. Now then: head north three screens (ignore the Heart
Container at F16, we need the Stepladder for it) and you'll be at D16 where the
beach makes a corner and you should see a -=DOCK=-. Walk straight to the dock
and keep walking as if you were going to pull a Jesus and walk on the water.
The Raft will appear automagically and take you across the water to a secret
cave at C16 (it looks like a Labyrinth entrance but it's not).

Head into the cave to find the Old Man again with the choice between a potion
and a -=HEART CONTAINER=-. Oh fine. You can pick the potion. EXCEPT NOT. Get
the Heart Container, you fool. Exit the cave and head back to the mainland,
then retrace your steps all the way back to the origin. From there, head north
one, then west all the way to the screen with the Potion Shop (G5), then north
three to the area with the Armos statues and the secret store where we bought
the Blue Ring.

Move the Armos again and go into the store. Buy the -=MONSTER BAIT=- from the
Merchant for 60 rupees and then return to the Overworld. Now head back south
to G5 (where the Potion Shop is) and head east one screen and then cross the
bridge. Head north immediately after crossing the bridge and walk off the dock.
The Raft will take you straight to the island where the Snake Labyrinth awaits
you. Enter.

   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 5                                     /                /__\

 \___________________________________________________________________________/
