-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   S L I P P E R Y   S N A K E                               [105-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H2 - You'll start once more at the bottom of the Labyrinth, so we'll be
working our way up. Before heading that way through, shoot left to H1.

-- H1 - Kill all of the Keese in here and a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the Key
and return to H2 before heading up to G2.

-- G2 - There will be three Vire in this room. Hit them to split them into Red
Keese and then pick off the Keese. One thing to be aware of with Vire is they
respawn every time you enter the room, unlike enemies from Labyrinth's past.
Once the room is cleared, use a key on the locked door to the right and head
through.

-- G3 - This room is very dark and contains obstacles that you cannon see.
You'll notice the -=COMPASS=- in the middle of the room and quite a few Vire
hopping about the room. You can use the Blue Candle to light these dark rooms
up, and there's about to be a lot of them. Kill the Vire and grab the Compass
and then make your way out of the maze and head to G2.

-- G2 - Kill the three Vire again and then head up through the next door.

-- F2 - Make Tippi proud and kill the swarm of Keese in this room. Pick up
whatever they drop and grab the -=KEY=- here. Proceed left to F1.

-- F1 - It's another dark room teeming with Vire who are conveniently not
bound by the obstacles that restrict you. Kill the Vire and continue through
the door at the top.

-- E1 - Another dark room, this time full of Zols. Kill the Zols and grab the
-=KEY=- in the middle of the room. Proceed through the door at the top.

-- D1 - And yet another dark room. Are we having fun yet? This time you've got
two Bubbles and three Vire to deal with. Once you've killed the Vire, we can't
go through the top door yet, so head through the locked door on the right.

-- D2 - LET THERE BE LIGHT! Finally, a room we don't have to light up. We've
got a room full of water, a singular path through it, and four Vire hopping
along that path. Take out the Vire one by one and once you've killed
everything, the door to the right will open.

-- D3 - Here we have two Bubbles, two Zols, and two Like Likes. This is our
first time encountering the Like Like, so be warned: if they touch you, they
will take your shield and you will not get it back unless you buy a new one. So
attack them with caution. Kill the Zols just to give yourself some breathing
room and then take notice of the two blocks in here. Push the leftmost block
one space to the left to reveal a staircase in the top right corner of the
room. Head down to the basement level. Kill the four Keese and then grab the
-=STEPLADDER=- from the platform on the right. Head back upstairs and go left
all the way over to D1.

-- D1 - You'll have to kill the Vire again. And now that we have the Stepladder
we can cross over the water gap. Head straight up to cross the gap and go
through the locked door to C1.

-- C1 - You can either kill the Vires here or ignore them, we just need to head
through the door to the right.

-- C2 - We're in another dark room and this one has the -=MAP=- in the bottom
right corner. Light the room up with the Blue Candle and skirt your way around
the edge of the room. As you can see, had we gone through the locked door in
D2, we'd have wasted a key and had to go around anyway. Once you have the map,
navigate back around the wall and bomb the top wall to create a doorway. Head
through to B2.

-- B2 - Here's a nice little rupee gift for you. Grab all the rupees and then
bomb the left wall and head through the new doorway to B1.

-- B1 - You'll immediately be assaulted by a Manhandla here. I guess it's a
miniboss? Fight it (don't forget that sweet bomb strategy) and kill it. Once
it's dead, the doors will open. Head through the top door to A1.

-- A1 - We've found the Old Man room and he's ready with another hint.

             "W A L K   I N T O   T H E   W A T E R F A L L ."

This is in reference to the waterfall at B11, the same waterfall above which we
got the White Sword. There's a cave there where you can pay the Old Man for a
hint. With that over with, use a key on the locked door to your right and head
to A2.

-- A2 - This room is dark again, though the Blue Candle isn't as necessary now
that we have the stepladder and can traverse these rooms as if there were no
gabs. Kill all of the Keese and grab the -=KEY=- from the middle of the room
before proceeding through the door to the right.

-- A3 - Watch out for the Traps as you enter! Skirt around the Traps and head
through the door at the bottom of the room.

-- B3 - There will be a lot more Vire (man, they really loved those guys for
this Labyrinth) so kill them off and then pay mind to the two blocks. You
should know what to do. Push the leftmost block left and the door to the right
will open. Head through to the boss chamber.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G L E E P G L O P   &   F L O O P D I E D O O S                   [105-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's that time again, the fourth boss of the game. Now I really hope you're
actually ready for a fight cause... well, Gleeok is also pretty easy. Let's get
ahead of him.
    _____________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G L E E O K   \_________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A huge dragon that has 2 to 4 heads and      | Received:              |
  |  spits out beams at Link. Heads that Link cuts |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  off from its body fly around in the air.      |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - In this specific case we're dealing with a two-head Gleeok. The two  |
  |    heads will shoot fireballs at you.                                   |
  |  - Once you separate a head, the head will turn red and fly around the  |
  |    room shooting fireballs at you.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Make sure you've got a decent bit of health going into the fight.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full health, use your sword beams from range to do the   |
  |    bulk of the work.                                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you don't, you'll have to get in close and just trade blows with  |
  |    him. Be consistent with your attacks and Gleeok will die before you  |
  |    do.                                                                  |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - I know that's not much of a strategy but don't blame me, blame the   |
  |    game designers.                                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gleeok is basically just a multi-headed, more annoying version of      |
  |  Aquamentus. Use your sword beams from range if you have full health,   |
  |  otherwise get in close and trade blows with it. You should be coming   |
  |  out the other side in no time.                                         |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
It may not have been pretty, but that double-headed dick is in the dirt. Once
it's dead, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- from the corner and head through the
door at the top. Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and you'll be teleported to
the Labyrinth entrance. Snake Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   P R E P A R I N G   T O   C O N T I N U E   M O R E               [CH5.3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Look at you. You're already halfway through the game. Four Labyrinths down,
four more to go. We'll be kicking Ganon in the nards before you know it. Now,
there are some things we can get to make our lives even more easy, so we'll
take a brief interlude from the Labyrinth smashing and run some worldly
errands.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 6                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      A BRIEF INTERLUDE      ___________________/   [CH106]      /\  /\
/__\/__\ __________________________/           \______________________ /__\/__\
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|        / Equipment \       / Heart Containers \        / Items \            |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|        Magical Sword            Container 5                                 |
|        Power Bracelet                                                       |
|                                                                             |
|                                                                             |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|                       / Sections Within This Chapter \                      |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|  [106-1]  Mo Heart, Mo Problems      - Grab the final Heart Container       |
|  [106-2]  I Have the Power!          - Get ripped                           |
|  [106-3]  Graverobber                - Level up your sword                  |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   M O   H E A R T ,   M O   P R O B L E M S                         [106-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alright. First things first, let's get that last Heart Container. We already
know where it is (F16), so let's make our way there. I promise you the path is
just so much easier to return to origin (H8) and head hard east like we have
repeatedly. The central squares are just so maze-like that you can easily get
twisted up sometimes. If you do decide to try and beeline it, take the raft
down and head hard east immediately. Stick to the top of the screen as you
progress through each grid because eventually you'll hit a screen where the top
half is separated. Once you reach the third screen with Moblins, take the
right-most path south. From here, you can push east to G16 and then up to F16.

Or just go to origin and do it that way. However you do it, once you get to
F16, clear out the Octoroks and use the Stepladder to cross the water and grab
-=HEART CONTAINER 5=-. And that's the last of the Overworld Heart Containers.
Now, count your hearts. You should have 12, which means we can get the Magical
Sword now! But first, we're going to grab the Power Bracelet since it's
somewhat on the way.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   I   H A V E   T H E   P O W E R !                                 [106-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Return to origin and make your way to the Potion Shop (G5). Now would be a good
time to buy some potion. Head west one screen to enter the Lost Woods and now
we're gonna cross it. So, head south first to H4. Take the bottom path west to
H3. There's not much else to do here but continue west to H2, so do that. Be
warned the Moblins can throw their spears through the bushes.

You'll be in a rocky area, so immediately head north and you'll be back in the
Lost Woods. Now then, this part of the Lost Woods is famously annoying. You
have to navigate it in a certain pattern or else you'll never get out of it.
The code to remember is ULDL, which means Up, Left, Down, Left. And you'll
quickly notice that each screen is the same. So, head up, then left, then down,
then left (or north, west, south, west). You'll know you've done it properly
when you get the Zelda puzzle solved chime and it spits you out in a new area
(coordinate F1). There are Lynels EVERYWHERE. Just avoid them for the most part
and head north to exit the Lost Woods and enter the Hyrule Graveyard.

Head north again up the stairs to a screen with actual tombstones. Ignore the
Ghinis (ghost guys floating around) and go east one, north one, and east one to
exit the Graveyard. Kill the Lynels here (arrows are your friend) and head east
another screen. Here we have a dozen Armos Statues and two staircases leading
up the mountain. Head up the staircase on the right and then head east one
screen and you'll find another arrangement of a dozen Armos Statues. We are now
at coordinate C5, which is where the Power Bracelet is located. Awaken the
Armos all the way on the right in the top row and the -=POWER BRACELET=- will
be underneath him. Use the map for help.

           _______________________________
          |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|
          |#|#|#|#|#|#|.'.|#|#|-|#|.'.|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯'-..'¯¯   ¯¯¯¯   ¯¯   ¯¯¯¯
                _     _     _     _     _        KEY:
               |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|   |P|
                                        ¯         P  - Power Bracelet
               |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|        A  - Armos
                ¯     ¯     ¯     ¯     ¯         #  - Rock
            _____.''-.__   _________   ____      |-| - Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|'.'|#|#|#|#|'.'|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Take your prize and enjoy your newfound strength. Now there's just one more
thing to do and it's nearby, fortunately.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G R A V E R O B B E R                                             [106-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we have 12 hearts, it's time to upgrade our sword once again. Make
your way back down the stairs and all the way west until you're back in the
Graveyard. Go north one screen and we're in the right coordinate (C2). The
tombstone you are looking for is middle row, third column. Use the map for
help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|%|%|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯|%|%|
                 |T|   |T|   |T|   |T| |%|%|     KEY:
                  _     _     _     _  |%|%|
                 |T|   |T|   |S|   |T| |%|%|      S  - Magic Sword
                  _     _     _     _  |%|%|      T  - Tombstone
                 |T|   |T|   |T|   |T| |%|%|      #  - Rock
            ___                        |%|%|      %  - Bush
           |#|#|                       |%|%|
           |#|#|                       |%|%|
            ¯¯¯                         ¯¯¯

Push the Tombstone up one space to reveal a staircase. Don't touch any other
Tombstones or it will spawn more Ghinis that can only be killed if you kill the
first Ghini!! Head on down to find the Old Man once more with another sword.

           "M A S T E R   U S I N G   I T   A N D   Y O U   C A N
                            H A V E   T H I S."

Take the Magical Sword off his hands and rejoice, for you've just doubled your
attack power! Now that we have the Magical Sword and all our other fixins, it's
time to tackle more Labyrinths.

Return to the origin point (trust me, Cage, it's the only way). When you get to
the Lost Woods part, just go north, east, south, east, north, east and you'll
be at the Potion Shop screen. From the origin point, go east one and then north
as far as you can go to C9 (with all the Peahats). BEFORE HEADING TO THE
LABYRINTH, let's make a quick detour. Head east to C14 (one past where we got
the third Heart Container), head north to B14 and then east two to B16. There's
a cave in a tree here (it's another Gambling Den) and a bunch of Peahats.
Ignore the cave and step one tile to the right of the tree and then walk up and
you'll take a secret staircase north into A16. Use the map for help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|#|~|
               \||   \|._.|    \||     |#|~|     KEY:
                ||/   ||G||/    ||/    |#|~|
                                       |#|~|      G  - Gambling Den
                   \||      \||  \||   |#|~|      #  - Rock
                    ||/      ||/| ||/  |#|~|      ~  - Water
            ___________________________|#|~|     |-| - Hidden Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

There's a cave on this screen as well. Head into the cave and grab the 100
rupees from inside. -=YOU NEED THESE 100 RUPEES SO MAKE SURE YOU EITHER DO THIS
OR HAVE 100 RUPEES=-. Now then backtrack all the way to C9 and then head west,
then north (and remember to watch out for falling Rocks as we make our way into
Death Mountain territory), then east until the screen starts repeating itself
(B12, a group of 10 rocks in the center with stairs leading up and stairs
leading down). Take the stairs up for four screens and you'll hear the puzzle
chime again and be face-to-face with the entrance to the Lizard Labyrinth. So,
go on in.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 7                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE LIZARD             ___________________/   [CH107]      /\  /\
/__\/__\ __________________________/           \______________________ /__\/__\

|        / Equipment \       / Heart Containers \        / Items \            |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|         Bomb Upgrade           Boss Container           Recorder            |
|                                                      Triforce Piece         |
|                                                                             |

|                       / Sections Within This Chapter \                      |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|  [107-1]  Breaking the Lizard        - Fight through the Labyrinth          |
|  [107-2]  Grab a Shovel              - Fight Digdogger                      |
|  [107-3]  Keeping On                 - Make your way to Dragon Labyrinth    |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

                               1     2     3     4
                                   ===== =====

                             ===== ===== ==x== =====

                       | M - Map                       |
                       | C - Compass                   |
                       | I - Item                      |
                       | B - Boss Fight                |
                       | T - Triforce Segment          |
                       | O - Old Man                   |
                       | # - Connected Stairs          |
                       | R - Rupee Room                |
                       | G - Hungry Goriya             |
                       | x - Locked Door               |
                       | + - Barricade Door            |
                       | ! - Bombable Wall             |

                       +-------------------------------+

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   B R E A K I N G   T H E   L I Z A R D                             [107-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H3 - You have two options here. Head to the right.

-- H4 - We have a new enemy to take down in this room: Pols Voice. Don't know
what the name has to do with the enemy but it's basically a bouncing rabbit's
head. And boy does it pack a wallop. Even with the Blue Ring, it'll ding you
for a full heart if you get hit. The Bow is excellent against them but
unfortunately, we need our rupees for now. So, toil away hacking them to death
with a sword and grab the -=KEY=- that drops once they're all dead. Now, bomb
the top wall and head through the hole.

-- G4 - It's the Old Man, and he's got a clue for us again.

           "D I G D O G G E R   H A T E S   C E R T A I N   K I N D S
                              O F   S O U N D ."

It's a nice hint for how to beat the boss considering the item we'll be getting
momentarily, but we'll get to that later. You'll notice that there's a locked
door to the left. If you've followed this guide the whole way, you should have
2 keys right now, because we had more than we needed in the Moon Labyrinth. So,
feel free to pop on through that locked door, or go all the way back around
through the Entrance screen if you'd like to save a key. Either way, get to G3.

-- G3 - Use the Blue Candle in here to turn the lights on. Across the partition
of water are some new enemies: Gibdos. They're basically just shambling mummies
that take a couple whacks with the sword a piece. Cross the water and cut them
down and grab the -=KEY=- that drops from one of them. Before continuing
through the door at the top, bomb the left wall and head through the opening.

-- G2 - There are another five Gibdos in here to deal with. Dispatch them
however you choose. One of them should drop some bombs, so make sure to pick
those up. Once they're all dead, the top door will still be sealed. And none of
these blocks do anything so don't bother trying. Instead bomb the left wall and
continue through the hole.

-- G1 - Enjoy the five Darknuts in this cramped space, it's a blast. Kill them
all with extreme prejudice and then focus your attention on the blocks. Push
the leftmost block up and go down the stairs. Kill the four Keese down in the
basement and then head up the other staircase which will take you to coordinate
A3.

-- A3 - There are two locked doors in here. We'll start with the one on the
left. Spend a key and head through the door.

-- A2 - Toil away in combat against the overwhelming number of Darknuts in here
and once you've killed them all, push the only block in the room up to reveal
a staircase in the corner of the room. Head down it. Kill the four Keese in the
basement and grab the -=RECORDER=- from the platform on the right. Return to A2
and head back right to A3.

-- A3 - Now we'll head down through the other locked door to B3.

-- B3 - Kill the swarm of Keese in this next room and grab the -=KEY=- that
rests at the center. Now bomb the right wall and head through the opening.

-- B4 - Here's the Old Man again, only this time he's not giving us a useless
hint. He's selling an upgrade to our bomb carrying capacity. Give him the 100
rupees I said to make sure you have, and your bomb capacity will be increased
to 12. He'll also do you a solid and replenish your bomb supply. Now backtrack
to the stairs and return to coordinate G1.

-- G1 - Ignore the five Darknuts here unless you just like pain and head back
through the hole in the right wall.

-- G2 - Kill the Gibdos here for a decent chance at hearts or rupees and then
head through the right wall again.

-- G3 - Kill the three Gibdos in here and the top door will open for us. It's
time to finally head through that door.

-- F3 - Get ready for another Miniboss. We're facing three Dodongos, but
remember they're a piece of cake and it's nothing to worry about. Just drop
your bombs in their path and watch as they blow themselves open. Remember that
you can slash them to death if your bomb misses slightly but the smoke stuns
them. Two bombs per Dodongo does them in and you should have plenty of bombs to
kill them all. Once they're all defeated, pick up any more bombs that you can
and go through the door to the left.

-- F2 - Cross the strip of water and kill all of the Zols in here. Once they're
all dead, a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the key and return through the right
door.

-- F3 - Now use a key on the locked door at the top and head through to E3.

-- E3 - Use the Blue Candle to light the place up so you can see, though to be
honest it's not entirely necessary. Grab the map and then head back down to F3.

-- F3 - And lastly, head through the door on the right to F4.

-- F4 - Use the Blue Candle again to light up this room. Kill all the Zols and
a five-rupee piece will appear in the middle of the room. Grab it and then head
through the door at the top.

-- E4 - There are five Gibdos wandering around in here. Kill them all and a
-=KEY=- will appear for you. Grab the key and then continue through the door at
the top.

-- D4 - Use the Blue Candle immediately to light the room up. There are three
Darknuts in here that you need to kill. Use the Stepladder to move in between
the sections of walkway and get easy angles on the Darknuts. When they've all
been killed, the -=COMPASS=- will appear in the center of the room. Grab the
Compass and continue through the door at the top.

-- C4 - There are two Pols Voices, two Gibdos, and two Keese in here for you to
slay. Feel free to use arrows to make the Pols Voices easier now that we've
gotten the bomb upgrade. So, give your enemies the ol' one-two and then grab
the -=KEY=- in the center of the room (if you didn't while fighting) and head
through the locked door to the left.

-- C3 - Kill the five Gibdos in here and grab the -=KEY=- that spawns on the
island once they're dead. Continue through the door to the left.

-- C2 - This is our last room before the boss! Kill the five Pols Voices (one
shots with arrows, don't forget) and then use a key on the locked door to the
left. Head through it to face Digdogger!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G R A B   A   S H O V E L                                         [107-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If at this point you're starting to feel like none of these bosses' names fit
them, well you're not alone. Now I really do genuinely hope that you are
seriously ready for a fight this time cause... well, Digdogger is pretty easy.
Let's dig up some dirt on him.
    __________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: D I G D O G G E R  \____________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "Big sea urchins. In spite of their big       | Received:              |
  |  bodies, they shrivel up when attacked. But    |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  watch out! They come on pretty strong."       |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Digdogger doesn't really have any attacks, it just constantly moves  |
  |    around the room. If it touches you, it will do damage.               |
  |  - Also watch out for the four statues in the corner that will be       |
  |    continuously shooting fire at you                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Digdogger's strategy makes him one of the easiest bosses in the      |
  |    game. Make sure you have your Recorder equipped and play it during   |
  |    the fight.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The Recorder melody will cause Digdogger to shrivel up to a tiny,    |
  |    much less threatening size. Once he's been shrunk down, two slashes  |
  |    with the Magical Sword will take him out.                            |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Digdogger moves pretty fast once it's been shrunk down. You can use  |
  |    the Boomerang to stun it and keep it in place while you whack at it. |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - You'll need to be evading the Stone Statue fireballs the entire      |
  |    time, cause they'll just keep peppering you. They're honestly a      |
  |    bigger threat that Digdogger.                                        |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Digdogger is a giant floating booger and a scaredy-cat. Play your      |
  |  Recorder to shrink it down and then hit it with a Boomerang and hack   |
  |  it to bits. A quick jam session and you'll be outta there in no time.  |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Well that was a tasty jam, but Digdogger didn't think so. Once it's dead, grab
the -=HEART CONTAINER=- from the corner and head through the door at the top
(don't worry about the door at the bottom, there's nothing in there). Grab the
-=TRIFORCE PIECE=- and you'll be teleported to the Labyrinth entrance. Lizard
Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   K E E P I N G   O N                                               [107-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We only have three more Triforce Pieces left to get. We're almost there, I feel
it in my plums. There's not much to do other than head straight for The Dragon
Labyrinth, so let's get to it. First things first, head down the stairs from
the entrance. Go immediately west when you get to the looping room to be back
at B11 with the Tektites and the Zola. Push west to B8 and cross the river with
the Stepladder to B7. Head west one more screen to B6 and take either of the
two staircases going south to C6. Once down them go west two screens to C4,
down some more stairs to D4, west one screen to D3, and then north up some
stairs to get to the Dragon Labyrinth entrance at coordinate C3. Kill the Lynel
up here if you want and then head into the Labyrinth.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 8                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE DRAGON             ___________________/   [CH108]      /\  /\
/__\/__\ __________________________/           \______________________ /__\/__\
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|        / Equipment \       / Heart Containers \        / Items \            |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|                               Boss Container           Magic Wand           |
|                                                      Triforce Piece         |
|                                                                             |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|                       / Sections Within This Chapter \                      |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
|  [108-1]  Dungeons & Dragons         - Fight through the Labyrinth          |
|  [108-2]  Curing Cancer              - Fight Gohma                          |
|  [108-3]  Let's-a-Go!                - Make your way to Demon Labyrinth     |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P

                             ===== ===== ===== =====

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   D U N G E O N S   &   D R A G O N S                               [108-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H2 - Once inside, immediately head right through the only open door in the
entrance.

-- H3 - Use the Blue Candle right away so you can see what's going on. There
will be a new type of enemy in here for you to do battle with: Wizzrobes, and
four of them. They are the worst enemy in this game (yes, even worse than
Darknuts). They teleport around the room shooting magic beams at you (that do a
ton of damage. The good part is they only shoot the magic beam after they
teleport and it's pretty easy to predict it and get out of the way in time then
give them a slash before they disappear again. Just play patient and kill them
one-by-one. One they're all dead, a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the key and head
up through the locked door.

-- G3 - It's the Old Man again and he has some more words for you.

             "A I M   A T   T H E   E Y E S   O F   G O H M A ."

It's a pretty simple one here. Gohma is the boss of this dungeon and her eyes
are her weak point. But for now, head back down to the entrance and now go left
through the locked door.

-- H1 - There will be some more Wizzrobes in here for you to kill. Defeat them
all and grab whatever then head up through the only other door.

-- G1 - Sometimes, after all the Wizzrobes and Darknuts, it's nice to just get
a room full of Zols. Kill all the Zols in here and the -=COMPASS=- will appear
in the center of the room. Grab it and continue up through the next door.

-- F1 - There will be a swarm of Keese in here and four Stone Statues in each
corner of the room. Dodge fireballs (poorly, if you're anything like me) while
you kill all of the Keese. Grab the -=KEY=- that drops after killing the last
Keese and head up through the next door.

-- E1 - Watch out for the Traps in this room! Just beeline straight up through
the next door and you should be fine.

-- D1 - Okay, this room is batshit. You've got two Red Wizzrobes, two Blue
Wizzrobes, three Like Likes, and two Bubbles. Avoid the Bubbles like the plague
since they'll render you incapable of using your sword for a few seconds.
Target the Wizzrobes first and try to get them out of the way. Once the
Wizzrobes have been dispatched, turn your attention to the Like Likes. Remember
to play keep away with these guys while you whittle them down, one touch and
your shield is gone. Just pray that one of them drops a Stopwatch. One they're
all dead (well, not the Bubble of course), push the leftmost block one space to
the left to open the doors. Continue up through the next door.

-- C1 - This room has more Wizzrobes and a tone of blocks to restrict your
movement while they can phase right through them. Kill them all and a five-
rupee piece will appear in the top right corner of the room. Instead of heading
up through the next door, bomb the right wall and move through the hole.

-- C2 - There's a bunch of Wizzrobes in here and it's dark. Use the Blue Candle
to light up the room. Kill all of the Wizzrobes (we'll come back through here
so it's best to just kill them now) and then grab the -=KEY=- from the island.
Use a key to head up through the locked door.

-- B2 - There's two Zols, two Bubbles, and two Like Likes in here. Take out the
Zols and the Like Likes and the -=MAP=- will drop. Grab the Map and then head
up through the locked door.

-- A2 - More Wizzrobes, yippee! Seriously, they suck ass. Kill them as fast as
you can, playing your best game of defense against the blue ones. When all of
the Wizzrobes are dead, push the left block to the left and a staircase will
open in the upper right corner of the room. Take the staircase down to the
basement, kill the four Keese, and grab the Magic Wand from the platform on
the right. Time to give these Wizzrobes a taste of their own medicine. Oh
wait, the Magic Wand doesn't hurt them. Head back upstairs and return to B2.

-- B2 - Head across the strip of water and through the door to the right.

-- B3 - There are five Red Wizzrobes in here. First, use your Blue Candle to
brighten up the room. Kill the Wizzrobes as they teleport and then grab the
-=KEY=- that is in the middle of the room. Continue up through the door across
the water.

-- A3 - There are two Like Likes, two Zols, and two Bubbles in here. For some
reason, not even the Magic Wand can damage a Bubble. Take out the Like Likes
and the Zols and then bomb the right wall in here and continue through the
hole.

-- A4 - It's the Old Man again with another hint! He's chock full of em now.

              "T H E R E   A R E   S E C R E T S   W H E R E
                  F A I R I E S   D O N ' T   L I V E ."

Alrighty then. I think what he means is that there are secrets out in the
world except for where there are Fairy Ponds. In which case, no duh. Thanks a
lot Old Man. Now, backtrack through A3, B3, B2, and then down to C2.

-- C2 - Head down through the door to D2.

-- D2 - Wizzrobes are so shitty that the Vires in here are gonna feel like
relief. Light up the room with your Blue candle. Take out the Vires (and
appreciate how they don't split into Red Keese with the Magical Sword) and then
continue through the door to the right.

-- D3 - Yet another room chuck full of pain-in-the-ass enemies. These rooms are
far worse than any boss fight in this game. You've got two Red Wizzrobes, two
Blue Wizzrobes, three Like Likes, and a Bubble. Make sure you've got your Bow
equipped for this. Start with the Red Wizzrobes to get the random teleportation
attack out of the equation. Then hammer the Like Likes with arrows to take them
out without getting close. Finally, do a dance with the Blue Wizzrobes and get
them gone. Once everything in the room is dead, push the sole block in here to
the left and a staircase will appear in the top right corner. Head down to the
basement and go up the other side to arrive at coordinate B6.

-- B6 - There are two Zols and two Like Likes in here along with two Bubbles.
Take the Zols and the Like Likes out and then head down through the door.

-- C6 - Use the Blue Candle to brighten this room up. Kill the three Vires in
here and a -=KEY=- will appear. Grab the key and continue left through the
door.

-- C5 - Watch out for Traps as you enter this room! There's a couple of Blue
Wizzrobes in here, they shouldn't give you too much trouble since their numbers
are small. Ignore the door to the south, it leads to a dark room with a
restrictive path full of Wizzrobes who give you bombs when you kill them all.
So, it's useless. Instead, proceed up through the locked door to the boss
chamber.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   C U R I N G   C A N C E R                                         [108-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gohma is actually my favorite boss in this game. She's got the best name, she's
got a cool design, and she feels the most Zelda-y out of them all. Though I do
have to wonder why there's literally two bosses who are dragons and yet the
crab is the boss of the Dragon Labyrinth. Oh well.

Now I seriously 100% hope that you are really ready for a fight this time
cause... well, Gohma is pretty easy. Like, Dodongo easy. After going toe to toe
with Wizzrobes, she's gonna feel like a piece of cake. Let's get Krabs.
    __________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G O H M A  \____________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "The super huge crab that lives in the        | Received:              |
  |  labyrinths. Its hard shell will repulse any   |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  attack. Attack its weak point with a special  |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |  weapon."                                      |                        |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Gohma will run back and forth at the top of her little lair and      |
  |    try to warm you up with some fireballs.                              |
  |  - That's pretty much it.                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Strafe and use your shield to block all of the incoming fireballs.   |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Wait for Gohma to descend from the top and open her eye, then shoot  |
  |    her in the eye with an Arrow. She'll die from one shot.              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you're out of rupees (and thus arrows), you literally can't use   |
  |    anything else, so find some rupees ASAP.                             |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gohma's a crabby bitch that hangs in the back and peppers you with     |
  |  fire. Teach her a lesson by shooting her in the eye with an arrow.     |
  |  You should be able to kill her almost as soon as you walk through the  |
  |  door so she's a quick one.                                             |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Poked her eye out like a Red Ryder BB Gun. Once she's dead, grab the -=HEART
CONTAINER=- she leaves behind and head through the door at the top. Grab the
-=TRIFORCE PIECE=- and you'll be teleported to the Labyrinth entrance. Dragon
Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   L E T ' S - A - G O !                                             [108-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Another Labyrinth, another Triforce Piece. Only two more left to get. So, let's
just head straight for the Demon Labyrinth, no time to waste. -=ALSO WE NEED TO
HAVE 100 RUPEES GOING INTO THE DEMON LABYRINTH=-. You also need to make sure
you have purchased the -=MONSTER BAIT=- from the Blue Ring shop, which you
should have already. And lastly, I'd pick up a Red Potion.

So, navigating to the Demon Labyrinth. It's a bit of a pain even though it's
three screens south from the Dragon Labyrinth. From the Dragon entrance: head
south down the stairs, then west into the graveyard. South one, west one, and
then south down the stairs. South one more time to enter the Lost Woods. Then
east one, north one, east one to get out of the lost part. If you chose to skip
the 100 rupees at the start of this guide, we can pause briefly here to grab
that now from this screen. Burn the -=TOPMOST=- bush in the single column that
bisects this screen and head down the stairs to grab the 100 rupees. Use the
map for help.

            _________     ___           ___
           |%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|    ¯ R|         |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|     |%|          ¯¯¯      KEY:
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯      |%|
                           |%|                    R  - 100 Rupees
            ___________    |%|_________           %  - Bush
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|___
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Now, head south one, east one, north two, and west one (either path, though top
is more convenient right now), then north one. You're here. To get here from
the origin point, you'll need to get back to the Lost Woods. So, from origin:
head north one and then west four to the start of the Lost Woods (G4). Don't
forget to grab a potion from the Old Lady on the way if you need to. Now head
north one, west one (either path, though top is more convenient right now),
then north one. You're here.

This square has a pond guarded by a Moblin and nothing else. WTF? Where's the
Labyrinth entrance? Have no fear. Equip your Recorder and play it. The pond
will dry up to reveal a flight of stairs: the entrance to the Demon Labyrinth.
Go on and head down.

     _______________                            __________________________
   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 9                                     /                /__\
 /\  /\      THE DEMON              ___________________/   [CH109]      /\  /\

|  [109-2]  Aquaman, Round Two         - Fight Aquamentus                     |
|  [109-3]  Stay the Course            - Make your way to Lion Labyrinth      |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P

                       | I - Item                      |

                       | # - Connected Stairs          |

                       +-------------------------------+

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   E X O R C I S T                                           [109-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H2 - We've got two options here starting out: up or to the right. We're
going to head right first.

-- H3 - This room will have two Moldorms for you to take out. Make short work
of them and then the door at the top will open. Head up through that door.

-- G3 - Use the Blue Candle in here to light the place up. Kill the swarm of
Keese and then head through the door to the right.

-- G4 - There's quite a few Blue Goriyas in here for you to contend with. Kill
them all and the door on the top wall will open. Go ahead through to F4.

-- F4 - It's the Old Man again!

            "T H E R E ' S   A   S E C R E T   I N   T H E   T I P
                           O F   T H E   N O S E ."

Alright. Head back to G4 and then immediately right to G5.

-- G5 - There's a Digdogger aided by four Stone Statues in here. You can kill
it if you want easily enough using the Recorder, but you can just bypass it
and continue through the door on the right.

-- G6 - There's eight Stalfos in here rattling around. Show them how brittle
their bones are and kill them all. One of them will drop a -=KEY=-, so pick
that up and then head back left all the way to G3.

-- G3 - Use the Blue Candle in here again. Make your way around to the top wall
and use a bomb to open a passageway. Head through to F3.

-- F3 - You'll need to use the Blue Candle in here as well. Then kill all of
the Stalfos and one of them will drop the -=COMPASS=-. Pick it up and then head
left through the door.

-- F2 - There's a plethora more Goriyas in here to deal with (both Red and
Blue), so take them out and then head left once more.

-- F1 - Here we have a Dodongo room with three Dodongos waiting to have their
guts bombed. Bomb them all to clear the room (remember either they eat the bomb
or the smoke stuns them and you slash away). Once they're all dead, continue up
through the locked door.

-- E1 - It's the Old Man again, this time with another Bomb Upgrade. Give him
your hard-earned 100 rupees and you'll walk away with a 16-bomb capacity now.
Can't beat that. If you don't have 100 rupees (I told you to), you can fight
the Stalfos and Goriyas around the Labyrinth to get more. Once you've got the
Bomb Upgrade, head back to F1 and then down to G1.

-- G1 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill all of the Keese in here and
they'll drop some bombs that you don't need. Continue down to H1.

-- H1 - There are two Stone Statues in here that will be constantly shooting
fireballs at you. Avoid or block the fireballs and grab the -=KEY=- in here
while dispatching the pesky Ropes. Once you have the key, backtrack all the way
up to G1, up to F1, right to F2, and then head up to E2.

-- E2 - There's going to be a two Goriyas, three Keese, and two Bubbles here
(I'll take this over Wizzrobes and Like Likes any day). Kill everything you can
kill in here and the door leading up will open. Head through it.

-- D2 - There's another Digdogger in here. It'll be easier if you kill this
one, but you can try to ignore it. All we need to do here is bomb the right
wall and head through to D3.

-- D3 - You'll find yourself in a desert room with two Moldorms to battle.
Dismantle them piece by piece and once they're dead, a -=KEY=- will appear.
Take the key and return to D2.

-- D2 - Shoot straight across left to D1.

-- D1 - The door will slam behind you and you'll be locked in with six Goriyas
(three Red and three Blue). Kill them all and a five-rupee piece will drop in
the corner. Grab it and then head up and use a key on the locked door.

-- C1 - This is a lot like an Old Man room except it's a Hungry Goriya. This
is the room we need the Monster Bait for, so I hope you picked it up. The
monster will hit you with "Grumble, grumble..." so swallow your fear and equip
your Monster Bait. Walk up to him and use the Monster Bait and he'll vanish
into thin air. Now you can proceed up to B1.

-- B1 - Use the Blue Candle to light this room up. Kill all of the Goriyas and
Keese in here while avoiding the Bubbles and then grab the map off the island.
Then make your way to the small platform at the top and bomb the top wall. Head
through.

-- A1 - Here's a nice little Rupee Room for you. Grab all the rupees in here
and then return to B1.

-- B1 - Once back in here, head right and use a key on the locked door. 

-- B2 - Kill all of the Goriyas in here, of which there are many, and then
continue up through the door.

-- A2 - There are more Goriyas in here (both Red and Blue this time). Kill them
all and a five-rupee piece will drop in the center. Grab your reward and
continue right through the next door.

-- A3 - There are four Stone Statues in the corners and Blue Goriyas
boomeranging about the room here. Kill the Goriyas and grab the -=KEY=- they
were guarding and then return promptly to through A2 to B2.

-- B2 - Instead of continuing to backtrack, bomb the right wall here to make a
passageway and head through.

-- B3 - There are a number of Goriyas in here and a blocked staircase. Kill all
of the Goriyas (use the magic wand or something with range to kill the ones
inside the blocks) and then push the leftmost block up to access the staircase.
Descend the stairs to the basement of this room. Kill the four Keese in here
and grab the Red Candle from the platform on the right to upgrade your candle
situation. Now you can use the candle as many times as you like in any room.
Return upstairs and bomb the right wall then continue through to B4.

-- B4 - There are six Blue Goriyas in here. Take them out and then continue
through the locked door to the right.

-- B5 - And lo, a third Digdogger room. This time we actually have to fight it.
So, whip out your Recorder and play a rocking tune and it will split into three
little Digdoggers. Stun them with your Boomerang and dice them up and the top
door will open. Head through it.

-- A5 - This room can kinda suck. There are two Stone Statues in the center of
the room and three Dodongos stomping about. Kill all of the Dodongos with bombs
and you'll also be rewarded with some bombs. Now bomb the right wall and head
through.

-- A6 - If the last room was difficult, this one is downright shitty. There are
a five  Wall Masters in this room and you'll actually have to kill them instead
of just avoiding them. And that can be tough. While you're trying to kill the
Wall Bastards, there are Bubbles floating about to make it even more annoying
for you. The good news, and there is good news, is that Wall Masters are one-
hit kills with your fancy-shmancy Magical Sword, so just don't get hit by a
Bubble when you're near a Wall Master and you should be alright. If you're
quick enough once you enter the room, you can spawn kill them all. Just head
directly to the top of the room towards the middle and they'll all spawn one-
by-one from the top wall. Kill them quickly before a Bubble comes up to ruin
your day. Once you've killed all five Wall Masters, you can push one of the
blocks in here. Use the diagram below to help you out.

                 _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 
                |_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|     KEY:
                                  |_|       
                                  |P|>    P - Push Block
                                  |¯|     > - Direction
                |¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|
                 ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯

Push the block and stairs will appear in the top right corner of the room. Make
your way around to the stairs (saying a prayer of thanks that Bubbles don't
take health away) and head down to the basement. Kill the four Keese in here
and head up the other set of stairs to appear in C2.

-- C2 - You'll be in a room full of Goriyas (both Red and Blue). Take them all
out to give yourself some peace and quiet and when you're ready, bomb the right
wall. Head through to the boss chamber.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A Q U A M A N ,   R O U N D   T W O                               [109-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We get to fight Aquamentus again. Guess they ran out of steam with the bosses
and said eff it. Now Aquamentus is embarrassed and has something to prove, so I
hope that you're ready for a fight cause... well, Aquamentus is pretty easy
again. Let's hit replay on his ass.
    _____________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: A Q U A M E N T U S   \_________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A type of dragon that some call a unicorn.   | Received:              |
  |  As well as having lots of attack power, it's  |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  a fearful opponent. It emits beams."          |  -- Triforce Piece 1   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Shoots a burst of three fireballs at you. Each fireball does a       |
  |    half heart of damage with the Blue Ring equipped                     |
  |  - That's it.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full heart containers going into the fight, just sit in  |
  |    the back and shoot sword beams at him. He'll die after a few hits.   |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The other strategy is to wait for him to fire a volley of fireballs, |
  |    dodge the projectiles, and then run up close and slash him. In my    |
  |    opinion, this is quicker and easier than shooting sword beams.       |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Beyond shooting fireballs, he barely even moves. He's a very         |
  |    stationary boss, so use that to your advantage when going in for     |
  |    the kill.                                                            |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Now that you have the Bow and Arrow, you can have some fun and kill  |
  |    him in three shots to the head.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Aquamentus is a very easy boss (even the second time). Shoot him with  |
  |  sword beams or wait for fireball volley and run up to slash him. You   |
  |  should be able to kill him without much fuss and get on to other       |
  |  things.                                                                |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Once Aquamentus has fallen, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- he leaves behind and
head through the door to the right. Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and
teleport to the entrance. Demon Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S T A Y   T H E   C O U R S E                                     [109-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Well, we've only got one Labyrinth left here: The Lion. We have nothing that we
need to do before heading that way so let's get to it. Head south one screen,
east two screens, and then south one screen and you'll be back at the Potion
Shop (G5). Be extra careful to keep all your hearts as you're going. While
we're here at G5, buy a Red Potion if you don't already have one.

Continue east one screen, north one screen, and then east eight screens (stick
to the top paths whenever there's a split), and south one screen (either path)
to G14. If you're navigating from the origin (H8): head east four screens
(H12) to the first area with water (where we got the first Heart Container),
north two screens, east along the top path then east again, and south one.

In this area (G14), you'll notice the screen is split into two sections by a
single wayward bush that's blocking the path through. Burn that bush with your
Red Candle to reveal a staircase: the entrance to the Lion Labyrinth. Descend
to your final trial before Death Mountain.

   /\               \__________________________/         ________________ /\
  /__\    Chapter 10                                    /                /__\

                           L A B Y R I N T H   M A P

                       +-------------------------------+

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   P A W ,   M E E T   T H O R N                                     [110-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H4 - At the entrance, we have three doorways to choose from. Head to the
right first.

-- H5 - Kill the Zols and the Keese in here and grab the -=KEY=- from the
island. Head back through H4 and continue left to H3.

-- H3 - There are two Stone Statues in the center of the room that will be
shooting fireballs at you while a Manhandla bounces around shooting more
fireballs at you. You have to kill the Manhandla to get the left door to open,
which we need open, so do your best to kill it quickly without losing too much
health. Once it's dead and the doors open, grab the five-rupee reward and head
through the left door.

-- H2 - There will be three Gibdos, two Red Darknuts, one Blue Darknut, and two
Bubbles in here. Avoid the Bubbles while killing everything else. I start with
the Gibdos and work from there because they might drop a Stopwatch which is
helpful with the Darknuts. If you still have full health (doubtful) you can use
sword lasers. Once everything is dead, push the leftmost block up to access the
stairs and head down to the basement. Kill the four Keese down here and grab
the Magic Book from the platform on the right. Return upstairs and go backtrack
to the entrance (H4).

-- H4 - Now that we have the Magic Book, our Magic Wand is even more powerful
(and thusly even more useful). Now then, continue up through the door to G4.

-- G4 - We're going to have to face another Manhandla. Kill it to get it out of
your way and then bomb the top wall and head through to F4.

-- F4 - Here we have five Darknuts and a Stone Statue in each corner. Talk
about some of our least favorite things. Ignore them for now (though we will
have to deal with them momentarily so brace yourself for that) and head through
the locked door on the right.

-- F5 - Use the Red Candle to give yourself some light here. There's a large
group of Pols Voices bouncing about so deal with them (arrows all the way) and
then grab the -=COMPASS=- from the middle of the room. Head back left to F4.

-- F4 - Momentarily has arrived and we now have to kill all the Darknuts in
here. Godspeed and do the best you can to not lose too much health to them.
Laugh at your own pain as the last one left seems to predict your every move
and take more hearts than the other four and the Statues combined. Once
they're all dead, the top and left doors will open, and they will drop a
-=KEY=-. Grab the key and head left.

-- F3 - Illuminate this room with the Red Candle as you enter. There will be
two Pols Voices, two Gibdos, and two Keese in here. Dispatch them however you
feel like and grab the -=KEY=- that drops when they're dead. Continue left to
the next room.

-- F2 - There are another four Stone Statues in here (seriously, these things
are annoying as hell) and three Red Darknuts. Avoid the fireballs and kill the
Darknuts while giving thanks that they aren't Blue ones. When they're dead a
-=KEY=- will drop. Pick it up and head back through F3 and up to E3.

-- E3 - In here is a Blue Gohma. It's just a little bit stronger than the Gohma
we took care of earlier. Why this miniboss version is stronger than the boss
version from two Labyrinths ago is well beyond me, but whatever. It takes three
arrows to put it down, so poke it in the eye and the door at the top will open
once it dies so continue up.

-- D3 - It's an Old Man room again and he's got a doozy for you.

          "S P E C T A C L E   R O C K   I S   A N   E N T R A N C E
                             T O   D E A T H ."

He's telling us how to get to Death Mountain with this one. So, take that
information and head back down to E3.

-- E3 - Now we're going to head right and use a key on the locked door.

-- E4 - There are three Gibdos, two Red Darknuts, one Blue Darknut, and two
Bubbles in here. Evade the annoying Bubble bastards and kill the rest, starting
with the Gibdos. Once everything's dead, you'll get a five-rupee reward. Grab
the money and run up through the locked door to D4.

-- D4 - Enjoy another room full of Blue Darknuts with two Stone Statues in the
center. Kill all the Darknuts as quickly (and painlessly) as you can and the
door to the right will open. Ignore it for now and bomb the top wall then go
through.

-- C4 - There is another Manhandla in here. Kill it using the usual method and
it will drop the -=MAP=- for us. I used my Potion for the first time after
this fight, so you have a metric. Grab the map and head through the locked door
above.

-- B4 - Now you'll face a Blue Gohma with four Stone Statues in the corner.
Enjoy attempting to discern which fireballs can be blocked by your shield and
which cannot. Kill the Gohma as quickly as you can and continue through the
door on the right.

-- B5 - In this room there are two Red Darknuts, two Blue Darknuts, and two
Pols Voices. Kill everything however you want to and then push the leftmost
block up to access the stairs. Head down to the basement and kill the four
Keese before grabbing the -=MAGIC KEY=- off the platform to the right. This
will change your key counter to "A", which stands for "All" I think, meaning
you can now open every locked door without needing to find more keys. Which is
nice, considering there's not that many more locked doors we'll need to be
opening now. Head back upstairs and back to B4.

-- B4 - The door above leads to a room full of enemies without a decent reward
so there's no point in heading up there. Just head back down through C4 to D4.

-- D4 - You'll have to kill the Blue Darknuts in here again (starting to see
why I said to have a Red Potion handy?). Kill them all as best you can and then
head to the right once the doors open.

-- D5 - There are two Red Darknuts, a Blue Darknut, two Gibdos, and two Bubbles
in here. You can ignore everything in here and beeline the stairs if you like.
In the basement, head up the other flight of stairs to F2.

-- F2 - There's a ton of Pols Voices in here. Kill them in a fit of roid rage
(use your bow) and ignore the -=KEY=- in the corner since we have the Magic Key
now (or grab it if you're slightly neurotic like me). Ignore the door on
the left and bomb the top wall. The next room is the boss chamber so use some
Potion if you're hurting and head through.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   R E I G N   O F   F I R E                                         [110-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Time for us to rematch the Gleeok, except this time he's got four heads. This
is the time when you should actually be ready for a fight cause... well, Gleeok
is still easy. More heads equals more deads.
    _____________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G L E E O K   \_________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A huge dragon that has 2 to 4 heads and      | Received:              |
  |  spits out beams at Link. Heads that Link cuts |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  off from its body fly around in the air.      |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - In this specific case we're dealing with a four-head Gleeok. The     |
  |    four heads will shoot fireballs at you.                              |
  |  - Once you separate a head, the head will turn red and fly around the  |
  |    room shooting fireballs at you.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Make sure you've got a decent bit of health going into the fight.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full health, use your sword beams from range to do the   |
  |    bulk of the work.                                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you don't, you'll have to get in close and just trade blows with  |
  |    him. Be consistent with your attacks and Gleeok will die before you  |
  |    do.                                                                  |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Now that we have the Magical Sword, it's two hits per head to        |
  |    decapitate.                                                          |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gleeok is basically just a multi-headed, more annoying version of      |
  |  Aquamentus. Use your sword beams from range if you have full health,   |
  |  otherwise get in close and trade blows with it. You should be coming   |
  |  out the other side in no time.                                         |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
Just goes to show that one brain is better than four. Once it's dead, grab the
-=HEART CONTAINER=- from the corner and head through the door at the top. Grab
the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and you'll be teleported to the Labyrinth entrance.
Lion Labyrinth complete!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G E T   R E A D Y   T O   G E T   R E A D Y                       [110-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Well, well, well. So, you completed all of the Labyrinths. Good job. But our
quest isn't over just yet. Now that we've forged the Triforce piece from it's
fragments, we're ready to take down Ganon. But we need to make sure we're
ready.

  -- Make sure to replenish your Red Potion.
  -- Make sure you have a full stack of 16 Bombs.
  -- Make sure you have at least 100 rupees for Arrows.

Once you meet all that criteria, you're ready to head to Death Mountain. Go
ahead and return to the origin point (H8) from the Lion Labyrinth entrance
since it's right next door. And from the origin: go east one, north five, west
one, and north one to enter the Death Mountain area. Now, cross the river and
head up the staircase. Go west two to a screen with two rocks. These are the
"Spectacle Rocks", cause the screen looks like a pair of glasses (a.k.a.
spectacles). Bomb the left rock at the -=BOTTOM MIDDLE=- to make a door. Use
the map for help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           '.''..'¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯'.|#|
                   .''-.       .''-.     |#|     KEY:
                 .'|#|#|'.   .'|#|#|'.   '.|

                 '.|#|9|.'   '.|#|#|.'   .-       #  - Rock
                   ¯¯          ¯¯¯¯¯     |#|

            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

That door is the entrance to Death Mountain, so head on in.
