-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Y O U ' R E   A L L   D O O M E D                                 [111-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Okay. The Big Kahuna. We got this. As you can see from the map, this is a much
more complicated Labyrinth that the others, so we're going to go piece by piece
and I'll break the map down for you as we move along.


                          6     7
                        ===== =====           KEY:
                    F  !  1  !  K  |    
                        ===== =====           E - Entrance
                    G        |  O  |          1 - Connected Stairs 1
                              =====           K - Key
                    H        |  E  |          O - Old Man
                              =====

-- H7 - Here we are, starting out. Only one direction to go so head up to G7.

-- G7 - Normally there'd be an Old Man here that tells you you're doomed and
should turn back. But since we've beaten all eight Labyrinths, he's not here.
Ignore the door to your left and continue straight ahead.

-- F7 - There are two Zols, two Like Likes, and two Bubbles in here. Avoid
them since all they drop for you is a key (and we have a Magic Key) and bomb
the left wall. Head through the opening.

-- F6 - In this room, we'll encounter Lanmolas for the first time. They're
basically Moldorms with an extra caveat. You can't damage their head (the one
section that looks different) until you've cut away the rest of their body.
Still, about as difficult as a Moldorm, which is not at all, and the Magical
Wand works wonders for them. So, kill them and push the leftmost block in here
up to access the stairs. Head down the stairs to the basement and kill the
four Keese down here then head up the other stairs to B5.


                  5     6     7     8
                      ===== ===== =====           KEY:
            A        |  2  !  O  |  I  |
                ===== ===== ==x== ==!==           1 - Connected Stairs 1
            B  |  1  x     |     |      |         2 - Connected Stairs 2
                ===== ==!== ===== ==!==           M - Map
            C        |     x     !  M  |          C - Compass
                      ===== ===== =====           I - Item
            D        |  C  |                      O - Old Man
                      =====

-- B5 - There's a whole lot of Like Likes in this room and your area is greatly
restricted, which fortunately hinders the Like Likes as much as it does you.
Kill the Like Likes quickly and don't let them get your shield! Head right
through the locked door.

-- B6 - Use the Red Candle in here to light the place up. There's three Blue
Wizzrobes starved for attention so leave them hungry and mad dash to the bottom
of the room. Bomb the bottom wall as quick as you can and move through.

-- C6 - There's two Like Likes, two Zols, and two Bubbles in here, and you'll
notice immediately the room is divided in three and you're in the middle path.
If there's any enemies in the path with you, kill them and then bomb the bottom
wall and head through.

-- D6 - There's three Blue Wizzrobes and a Red Wizzrobe in here. Kill them all
and the last one will drop the -=COMPASS=- for you. Grab and make your way back
to B6.

-- B6 - Keep ignoring the Blue Wizzrobes in here and hurry through the door to
the right now.

-- B7 - This room also has a new enemy in it. A Patra, which is a blue flying
thing surrounded by smaller flying things. But we can ignore it for a moment
and hurry out through the bottom door.

-- C7 - Ah, the sweet simplicity of Gels. Kill them off if you want and bomb
the wall on the right. Head through the new hole.

-- C8 - Another Patra here and this time we have to fight it. The way to kill
a Patra is by first killing all of the little flying things that spin around

it. You cannot damage the actual Patra until the little buggers around it have
all been destroyed. And they take two hits head to get rid of. Once they're
all gone, it takes three hits to destroy the central guy. Once you've killed
this Patra (and hopefully not lost too many hearts, the -=MAP=- will drop for
you. Grab it and then bomb the north wall in here and continue through the
hole.

-- B8 - There's two Blue Wizzrobes, two Red Wizzrobes, three Like Likes, and a
Bubble in here. If that sentence didn't make you roll your eyes, nothing will.
The good news is that you can largely ignore them as you bomb the north wall
and head through, just watch your back with the Like Likes.

-- A8 - There's a plethora of Blue and Red Wizzrobes in here. Kill them all
while trying not to lose hearts. Once they're all dead, push the leftmost block
up to access the stairs and head down to the basement. Kill the four Keese down
here and grab the -=RED RING=- from the platform on the right. This will reduce
our incoming damage by another factor of 2 (factor of 4 total from base
incoming damage). Head back upstairs and backtrack to B7.

-- B7 - Now it's time to kill the Patra, though it's much less of a threat to
our health now that we have the Red Ring. Take it down like you did the last
one and then head up through the locked door.

-- A7 - The Old Man is in here and he's got a cryptic message for us.

                 "G O   T O   T H E   N E X T   R O O M ."

But there's no other doors... Could it be? Yes, it could. Bomb the wall to the
left and continue through the hole.

-- A6 - There two Red Wizzrobes and three Blue Wizzrobes in here. Kill them all
and then turn your attention to the two blocks in here. You should know what to
do by now. Push the left block left to reveal a staircase in the top right
corner. Head down it to the basement and kill the four Keese. Then head up the
other staircase to G4.


                     2     3     4        KEY:
                   ===== ===== ==x==
               G  | 3 K |     x  2  |     2 - Connected Stairs 2
                   ===== ===== ==x==      3 - Connected Stairs 3
                                          K - Key

-- G4 - There's six Zols in here. Kill them all and grab whatever they drop
before heading through the locked door to the left.

-- G3 - There's a swarm of Keese in here. Kill them all if you want five
rupees, otherwise continue through the door to the left.

-- G2 - Admire the Patra's new moves briefly and then kill it unceremoniously.
Once it's dead, push the leftmost block up to access the staircase. Head down
to the basement and kill the four Keese down here. Head up the other staircase
to C1.


                           1
                         =====         KEY:
                     B  |  I  |
                         ==!==         3 - Connected Stairs 3
                     C  |  3  |        I - Item
                         =====

-- C1 - There's three Blue Wizzrobes and two Red Wizzrobes in here. Kill them
all to get them out of your way and then bomb the top wall. Head through to B1.

-- B1 - There's three Blue Wizzrobes, two Red Wizzrobes, and three Bubbles in
here. Do your best with the bubbles while you kill the Wizzrobes. Once
everything is dead, use the diagram below to determine which block to push.

                 _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 
                |_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|     KEY:
                                  |_|       
                                  |P|>    P - Push Block
                                  |¯|     > - Direction
                |¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|
                 ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯

Once you push the block, a staircase will appear in the top right corner. Make
your way around the blocks to the stairs and head down to the basement. Kill
the four Keese and grab the Silver Arrow from the platform on the right. Head
back upstairs and back down to C1.

-- C1 - Push the leftmost block up to access the stairs and head down to the
basement. You'll have to kill the Keese again then head up the other stairs
back to G2.


                      1     2
                    =====
                D  |  4  !
                    ==x==               KEY:
                E  |     |
                    ==x== ==+==         3 - Connected Stairs 3
                F  |     +     |        4 - Connected Stairs 4
                    ===== =====
                G        |  3  |
                          =====

-- G2 - Once you're back in G2, head up to F2.

-- F2 - There are six Like Likes in here. Use the Magic Wand to kill them from
range (or sword beams if you have full health) and once they're all dead, the
door to the left will open. Continue to the left.

-- F1 - You'll be in a dark room with five Zols. If you kill one with your
upgraded Magic Wand, the fire will light the room up and you won't have to
switch to the Red Candle. Kill the rest and then head up through the locked
door.

-- E1 - There will be two Blue Wizzrobes and two Red Wizzrobes in here and
you'll be pretty limited in your movement options. You can skip them or kill
them, doesn't matter, just continue up through the next locked door.

-- D1 - Watch out for the Traps as you enter! There's two Blue Wizzrobes and a
Red Wizzrobe in here. Kill them quickly. Then push the left block to the left
and some stairs will appear in the right corner under the trap. Bait it into
moving and then head down the stairs to the basement. Kill the Keese down here
and then head up the other stairs to A5.

 
                      4     5         KEY:
                    ===== =====
                A  |  5  !  4  |      4 - Connected Stairs 4
                    ===== =====       5 - Connected Stairs 5

-- A5 - There's two Red Wizzrobes and two Blue Wizzrobes in here and Traps in
the corner. Do your best to kill the Wizzrobes without taking too much damage
and then bomb the wall on the left. Head through to A4.

-- A4 - There are two Zols, two Like Likes, and two Bubbles in here. Dodge the
bubbles as you take out the rest, after all you're a pro now. Once everything's
dead, push the leftmost block up and head down the stairs to the basement. Kill
the four Keese and head up the other stairs to F3.


                        3
                      =====
                  D  |  Z  |        KEY:
                      ==+==
                  E  |  B  |        5 - Connected Stairs 5
                      ==+==         B - Boss (Ganon)
                  F  |  5  |        Z - Princess Zelda
                      =====

-- F3 - There is another Patra in here. Kill it and the door at the top will
open, which leads to Ganon's room. Drink a potion if you have one and equip
your Bow with the Silver Arrows now. When you're ready, head through the door.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   M A X I M U M   E F F O R T                                       [111-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And just like that we're at the last boss. Feels like just this morning we
started this whole adventure, probably cause it was very likely actually this
morning. But alright, I know we've messed around before, but this time I really
for real hope that you're ready for a battle cause... well, Ganon is also easy.
Let's roast this pig.
    ___________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G A N O N   \___________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  ""Link's going to have a difficult time       | Received:              |
  |  trying to destroy Ganon. He's real mean. But  |  -- Princess Zelda     |
  |  even Ganon has his weak point.                |  -- Triforce           |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Disappears and shoots unblockable fireballs at you.                  |
  |  - That's it.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - You CAN walk on the black parts of this room. The tiles are just for |
  |    decoration. The whole room is solid.                                 |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - While Ganon is fighting like a bitch and being invisible, you gotta  |
  |    find him. Stab blindly around the room until you hit him. He'll      |
  |    appear briefly and then disappear again. Do this four times.         |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - After the fourth hit, Ganon will turn brown-ish and that's your      |
  |    cue. Shoot him with a Silver Arrow and he'll turn to ash.            | 
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Ganon's a chump. Whack around blindly with the sword until you hit him |
  |  four times then shoot him with a silver arrow. He's no real threat at  |
  |  all which kinda leaves you wondering how Hyrule ever got into this     |
  |  mess in the first place.                                               |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
David beats Goliath every time. Once Ganon's dead, grab the -=TRIFORCE=- from
his pile of ashes and head up through the door. It's Princess Zelda! And she's
imprisoned by fires! Cut down the fires with your Magical Sword to free Zelda
and beat the game! CONGRATULATIONS!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G R A N D   F I N A L E                                           [111-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

            "T H A N K S   L I N K,   Y O U ' R E   T H E   H E R O
                             O F   H Y R U L E ."

      "F I N A L L Y ,   P E A C E   R E T U R N S   T O   H Y R U L E .
                   T H I S   E N D S   T H E   S T O R Y ."

That's it, you've done it. Zelda and Link will hold up their Triforce pieces in
triumph. Good has won the day today. Or has it? After the credits, you'll see a
pesky little piece of Triforce in Ganon's ashes.

         "A N O T H E R   Q U E S T   W I L L   S T A R T   F R O M
                                H E R E .

              P R E S S   T H E   S T A R T   B U T T O N." 

                              .-----------.
                             |  S T A R T  |
                              '-----------'

Well... What are you waiting for?

 \___/
     
Now then, the Second Quest. It's honestly quite a bit more difficult than the
First Quest, but it's still an enjoyable experience and not too much trouble if
you keep your wits about you and do it in the proper order (which conveniently,
I'm about to help you do).

The dungeons are different, the bosses are different, the items are jumbled up,
and the difficulty is upped a bit. An interesting added mechanic the we'll
encounter are "illusion walls" that will sometimes work both ways or only work
one way.

Additionally, if you follow this guide exactly, you'll have more than enough
keys (just like in First Quest). If you choose to explore, try not to use a lot
of keys. NEVER BUY KEYS.

And lastly, there are three new enemies that we will encounter: Red Bubbles
(disables your sword PERMANENTLY), Blue Bubbles (gives your sword back), and
Electric Ropes (just like regular ropes but electrified).

Once again, the strategy I present below is, in my opinion, the best strategy
to beat The Legend of Zelda, Second Quest. Follow it faithfully or use it when
you need it, entirely up to you. Let's get this show on the road.

|  [201-6]  Get 2 Steppin'              - Off to the E Labyrinth              |
 \___________________________________________________________________________/


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S T A R T I N G   O U T                                           [201-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You'll notice quickly that things are quite different this time around. Most of
the Overworld has stayed the same (though the locations of most things have
changed), while you'll see soon that the Labyrinths have been completely
redone.

Welcome to Second Quest! It's harder (and more fun I think) and I'll be your
tour guide this evening. So, let's kick things off by heading to the cave at
our origin coordinate (H8).

            "I T ' S   D A N G E R O U S   T O   G O   A L O N E!
                            T A K E    T H I S."

The Old Man will give you a -=WOODEN SWORD=-. If you thought it was bad the
first time around, wait until you actually have to use it through a Labyrinth.
But before we can get to that, there's some things we need to do.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A N   O L D   F L A M E                                           [201-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The first item on our shopping list is the Blue Candle once again. So, we need
to get 60 rupees to afford our bush burner once again. So, we're going to kill
some enemies until we have bombs and hit some hidden places. Make your way hard
east all the way to H16, killing everything along the way. Something should
drop bombs for you. If they don't, head up to G16 and buy some bombs from the
Shop there since you should at least have 20 rupees. Now, we're just going to
follow the coast north three (from G16), west one, north one, west one. And
we're at C14. Bomb the north-most wall on the -=MIDDLE TILE=-. Use the map for
help.

            ___   _______     _____________
           |#|#|-|#|#|#|#|   |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           |#|#|-|#|#|R|.'   | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |#|#|-|#|¯        |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           |#|#|-|#|         | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |     KEY:
           |#|#|-|.'          \ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
            ¯¯¯                ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯       R  – 30 Rupees
                                                  #  - Rock
                                                  ~  - Water
            ___________       _____________      |-| - Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|'.   |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|   |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Grab the 30 rupees from inside and then immediately head south one screen to
D14. Move the Armos on the right to reveal a staircase. Head down and grab the
30 Rupees from inside. Now that we have 60 rupees, we can return to the origin
and head to G7 (north one, west one) and buy the Blue Candle.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   F A R M I N G   S I M U L A T O R   1 9 8 6                       [201-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

That wasn't too bad. Well, it's about to be. We now need to get 250 rupees to
pick up the Blue Ring. It's more necessary now that it was before, so we have
no choice. Since we have the Blue Candle we can go ahead and pick up the ONLY
100-rupee gift on the map in Second Quest. For that, we need to make our way to
F4.

So, head east three screens (past the Potion Shop) to G4 and the Lost Woods,
then head north one to F4. Use the Blue Candle to burn the -=BOTTOM LEFT=-
green bush here. Use the map for help.

            _____________     _____________
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|%|%|
           |%|%|        _               ¯|%|     KEY:
           |%|%|       |%|      _         ¯
           |%|%|        _      |%|                R  - 100 Rupees
           |%|%|        R|      ¯         _       %  - Bush
           |%|%|        ¯               _|%|
            _______     _       _   _  |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|   |%|     |%| |%| |%|%|
           |%|%|%|%|   |%|     |%| |%| |%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯       ¯   ¯   ¯¯¯

Head down the revealed stairs and grab the 100 rupees. After we grab that
though, there's not much else we can grab. So, we have to farm rupees. We have
two options for doing that.

1. Run our farming loop from H9 to H16 to H12 to G12 to G9 and then back
around. This is a great way to get a bunch of rupees, especially if you can
continue to get a bunch of kills without taking damage as every 10th kill will
drop a five-rupee piece guaranteed.

2. Use the second controller to save the game and play the Gambling Game at
H7 over and over until we have 255 rupees. Probably the faster of the two
options but does involve continuously saving and retrying if luck doesn't go
your way.

However you want to do it, farm rupees until you're maxed out at 255 and then
we need to make our way to A16 (where we got a 100-rupee gift in First Quest).
So, from origin: head east one, north five, east five, north one, east two to
B16. If you got the 100-rupee gift, you should recognize this area. There's
a secret path on the north wall just to the right of the cave. Use the map for
help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|#|~|
               \||   \|._.|    \||     |#|~|     KEY:
                ||/   ||G||/    ||/    |#|~|
                                       |#|~|      G  - Gambling Den
                   \||      \||  \||   |#|~|      #  - Rock
                    ||/      ||/| ||/  |#|~|      ~  - Water
            ___________________________|#|~|     |-| - Hidden Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|~|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Take the secret path up to A16 and enter the cave here. Inside is the fourth
Shop with the -=BLUE RING=-! Buy the Blue Ring and listen to the game laugh at
you as all your rupees ding away. But don't worry, you got the good end of
the deal.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A I N ' T   A F R A I D   O F   N O   G H O S T S                 [201-4]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we have the Blue Ring, we should get the one Heart Container that we
can actually find right now. To do that, we need to get to Hyrule Graveyard,
specifically coordinate C1. So, from A16: head back down the steps, then west
two, south one, west five, south four, west five (into the Lost Woods), south
one, west two (along bottom path), and then north one in to G2, the actual Lost
Woods screen.

Remember the code here: ULDL (up, left, down, left) and head those directions
to go west one more to G1. Head north four from here to the top left screen of
the Graveyard. The tombstone we need to move is -=SECOND COLUMN, MIDDLE ROW=-.
Use the map for help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|.'_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯_¯¯¯¯¯¯ 
           |#|#| |T|   |T|   |T|   |T|           KEY:
           |#|#|  _     _     _     _
           |#|#| |T|   |H|   |T|   |T|            H  - Heart Container
           |#|#|  _     _     _     _             T  - Tombstone
           |#|#| |T|   |T|   |T|   |T|            #  - Rock
           |#|#|                        ___
           |#|#|                       |#|#|
           |#|#|                       |#|#|
            ¯¯¯                         ¯¯¯

Push the Tombstone up and head down the stairs to find the Old Man. He will
give you the choice between a Red Potion or a -=HEART CONTAINER=-. Didn't we go
through this in the First Quest? Pick the Heart Container. Jeez. That will
bring us up to a whopping four hearts. Whoopty doo, Basil.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   B E C O M I N G   P O W E R   M A N                               [201-5]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And now, for our last errand, we need to get the Power Bracelet. This is more
of a while we're in the area errand and less of a necessity. So, let's head
south one, east three, north one (right staircase), and east one. Move the
top right Armos here to reveal the -=POWER BRACELET=-. Use the map for help.

           _______________________________
          |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|
          |#|#|#|#|#|#|.'.|#|#|-|#|.'.|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯'-..'¯¯   ¯¯¯¯   ¯¯   ¯¯¯¯
                _     _     _     _     _        KEY:
               |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|   |P|
                                        ¯         P  - Power Bracelet
               |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|   |A|        A  - Armos
                ¯     ¯     ¯     ¯     ¯         #  - Rock
            _____.''-.__   _________   ____      |-| - Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|'.'|#|#|#|#|'.'|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Grab the Power Bracelet and shapow! You're a bunch stronger and stuff! 

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G E T   2   S T E P P I N '                                       [201-7]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And that's all we have to do for now. It's time to make our way to the first
Labyrinth. Fortunately, this one is in the same location as First Quest.
Unfortunately, it's a bit of a pain in the ass to get to from here. We
basically have to get all the way back around to the origin and head up from
there (there is LITERALLY no other way). So, head back to the origin (H8).

From the origin, head: east one, north four, and west one across the bridge.
Enter the cave here to start the E Labyrinth.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   E   I S   F O R                                                   [202-1]
   E E L L O G O F U S C I O U H I P O P P O K U N U R I O U S 
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H1 - From the entrance, we have two options: up or right. We're going to
head right first.

-- H2 - Kill the five Red Goriyas in here and the -=BOOMERANG=- will appear for
you. Take it, then return to the entrance and head up now.

-- G1 - Kill the three Red Goriyas in here while dodging fireballs from the two
Stone Statues in the middle. When the Goriyas are dead, take the -=KEY=- they
drop. Bomb the right wall (remember, we always bomb the middle of the wall in
Labyrinths) but don't go through just yet. Instead, head up.

-- E1 - Kill the Stalfos in here (careful, they now throw their swords as well)
and they'll drop the -=COMPASS=-. Grab it and continue up to D1.

-- D1 - Killing the three Blue Goriyas in here will drop bombs for you. Feel
free to skip and continue up to C1.

-- C1 - Killing all of the Gels in here will drop five rupees for you. Feel
free to skip and head right through the locked door.

-- C2 - MINIBOSS - Dodongo. You know how to kill it. Bomb its guts out and the
sealed door at the bottom will open. Continue through to D2.

-- D2 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill the four Keese in here to open
the door from where you came. Then grab the map from in here and backtrack all
the way to G1 where you bombed the wall.

-- G1 - Head through the bomb opening now.

-- G2 - Kill the five Keese in here and then push the leftmost stone to access
the stairs in here. Head down and kill the four Keese then continue up the
other side.

-- B2 - You'll face three Bubbles and some Wall Masters. Kill all of the Wall
Masters and they will drop a -=KEY=- (if you can find an area where they spawn
from the wall, you can stand beside it and spawn kill them, just watch out for
the Bubbles). Take the Key and continue left.

-- B1 - It's not necessary to kill the three Blue Goriyas in here. Just avoid
the fireballs from the Stone Statues and bomb the top wall, then head through
the hole to face the first Boss.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   I T ' S   M E N T A L                                             [202-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Well, that was quick. We're already facing the first boss and it should be a
familiar foe if you didn't skip straight to Second Quest. Aquamentus the fire-
breathing dragon. Now, I hope you're ready for a fight cause... well, he's more
of a nuisance than anything. With the Wooden Sword, he's just kind of annoying,
but I wouldn't say hard. So, let's fire him.
    _____________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: A Q U A M E N T U S   \_________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A type of dragon that some call a unicorn.   | Received:              |
  |  As well as having lots of attack power, it's  |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  a fearful opponent. It emits beams."          |  -- Triforce Piece 1   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Shoots a burst of three fireballs at you. Each fireball does a       |
  |    half heart of damage with the Blue Ring equipped                     |
  |  - That's it.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full heart containers going into the fight, just sit in  |
  |    the back and shoot sword beams at him. He'll die after a few hits.   |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The other strategy is to wait for him to fire a volley of fireballs, |
  |    dodge the projectiles, and then run up close and slash him. In my    |
  |    opinion, this is quicker and easier than shooting sword beams.       |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - With the Wooden Sword, he will take six hits to put down.            |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Beyond shooting fireballs, he barely even moves. He's a very         |
  |    stationary boss, so use that to your advantage when going in for     |
  |    the kill.                                                            |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Aquamentus is a very easy boss (not surprising considering he's the    |
  |  first boss of the game. Shoot him with sword beams or wait for         |
  |  fireball volley and run up to slash him. You should be able to kill    |
  |  him without much fuss and get on to other things.                      |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

Once he's fallen, grab your -=HEART CONTAINER=- reward and continue through the
door to the right. Pick up the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- and you'll be warped out of
the dungeon.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   W H I L E   W E ' R E   H E R E                                   [202-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Not so bad, right? And now that we have five hearts, we can go ahead and
upgrade to the White Sword and ditch this Wooden turd. From the entrance to the
E Labyrinth, head: east one, north one, west one, north one (watch out for
Rocks now), east four, and then north up the stairs. Enter the cave here and
you'll find the Old Man once again.

           "M A S T E R   U S I N G   I T   A N D   Y O U   C A N
                            H A V E   T H I S."

And master we have, so take the -=WHITE SWORD=- and rejoice, for you're no
longer a scrub and I don't want no scrubs. Once you have the White Sword, we
should go ahead and pick up the Magical Shield so we can block all these damn
fireballs. So, return to the Overworld and head south one, west four, south
one, east one, south two (if you need rupees, there's a 30-rupee gift here (E9)
if you burn the topmost bush you can in the three columns on the right. Use
the map section if you can't find it.), and west two. We're going to burn the
-=CORNER BUSH=- here for Shop 3 (same as in First Quest). Use the map for help.

            _______________________________
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|      KEY:
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~_________________|
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|                        S  - Shop 3
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |    _____________       %  - Bush
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|    S|%|%|%|%|%|%|      ~  - Water
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
           | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |   |%|%|%|%|%|%|%|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯     ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Head into the shop and buy the -=MAGICAL SHIELD=- for 90 rupees. Now return to
the Overworld and we're ready to head to the A Labyrinth, which is conveniently
nearby. Head south one, west one, south one, west one, north three and we're
here: D5, where the Blue Ring was in First Quest. Now, move the -=TOP MIDDLE=-
Armos to reveal the stairs down. Use the map for help.

            _______________________________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|.'¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|#|#|
           |#|  _   _   _              '.|#|     KEY:
           |#| |A|  2| |A|               |#|
           |#|      ¯          __________|#|      2  - Labyrinth Entrance
           |#| |A| |A| |A|    /~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |      A  - Armos
           |#|  ¯   ¯   ¯    |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|      #  - Rock
           |#|'.___________  | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |      ~  - Water
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#| |~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#| | ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ |
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

Head down the stairs to enter the A Labyrinth.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   W H A T ' S   T H E   A   S T A N D   F O R ?                     [203-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H1 - Not much to do here at the entrance, so head up through the only door.

-- G1 - Kill the five Gibdos in here and they will drop a -=KEY=- for you.
Continue up since that's still the only way you can go.

-- F1 - Kill the three Zols in here and push the left stone to open the door
where you came from. Now continue through the locked door on the right.

-- F2 - Kill the three Red Darknuts in here and the -=COMPASS=- will appear.
Grab it and immediately return to F1 before continuing up.

-- E1 - Either kill or ignore the Keese in here and get the -=KEY=- while
avoiding the fireballs from the two Stone Statutes. Continue up to D1.

-- D1 - The door will shut behind you as you enter. Kill the four Gibdos in
here to open it once more. Now continue up to C1.

-- C1 - Kill the Keese and the door up will open. Before continuing that way,
bomb the right wall. Head through the hole.

-- C2 - Ignore the Keese in here and grab the -=KEY=- in here, then return to
C1 before heading up to B1.

-- B1 - MINIBOSS - Manhandla. Kill the Manhandla (try your best with the one-
bomb-kill strategy) and it will drop a -=KEY=- for you. Take the key and head
right.

-- B2 - There's five Red Darknuts in here so take them out and head up through
the locked door.

-- A2 - Watchout for Traps as you enter! Kill the two Zols in here and take the
-=MAP=-. Head back down to B2 and then continue down to C2.

-- C2 - Head straight down through this room and through the bottom wall
(illusion wall).

-- D2 - Head down the stairs here and kill the four Keese. then take the
-=RECORDER=- from the platform on the right. Head back upstairs and go through
the left illusion wall (this wall is one-way).

-- D1 - You'll have to kill the Gibdos in here again. Then head down two and
right one.

-- F2 - We're back in the Compass room. Kill the three Darknuts again if
they're back. Bomb the top wall and continue through.

-- E2 - There's two Gibdos, two Pols Voices, and two Keese in here. Kill them
all and they'll drop another -=KEY=- for you. Take the key and continue right.

-- E3 - The five Darknuts in here will drop bombs for you. Kill them if you
need some and then continue down to F3.

-- F3 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill all the Keese in here and a
-=KEY=- will appear. Take it and continue down.

-- G3 - The door will slam shut behind you. Kill the three Zols in here to open
the doors and a -=KEY=- will drop. Grab the Key and continue down.

-- H3 - Kill all the Gibdos in here and they will drop five rupees for you.
Sweet, you're less poor. Head down the stairs in here. Kill the Keese in the
basement and continue up the other stairs.

-- D3 - Kill the three Darknuts in here to get some more bombs. Head through
the locked door at the top to face the Boss.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   N O T   F E E L I N G   V E R Y   G L E E F U L . . .             [203-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Boss numero dos. And it's not Dodongo, so already things are changing order.
We're actually facing a three-headed Gleeok this time, so I hope you're ready
for a fight now cause... well, he's a chump. Let's head on in.
    _____________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G L E E O K   \_________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A huge dragon that has 2 to 4 heads and      | Received:              |
  |  spits out beams at Link. Heads that Link cuts |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  off from its body fly around in the air.      |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - In this specific case we're dealing with a two-head Gleeok. The two  |
  |    heads will shoot fireballs at you.                                   |
  |  - Once you separate a head, the head will turn red and fly around the  |
  |    room shooting fireballs at you.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Make sure you've got a decent bit of health going into the fight.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full health, use your sword beams from range to do the   |
  |    bulk of the work.                                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you don't, you'll have to get in close and just trade blows with  |
  |    him. Be consistent with your attacks and Gleeok will die before you  |
  |    do.                                                                  |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - I know that's not much of a strategy but don't blame me, blame the   |
  |    game designers.                                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gleeok is basically just a multi-headed, more annoying version of      |
  |  Aquamentus. Use your sword beams from range if you have full health,   |
  |  otherwise get in close and trade blows with it. You should be coming   |
  |  out the other side in no time.                                         |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

As always with Gleeok, it's a battle of attrition. So, once he's been worn out,
grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- and continue up through the next door. Grab the
-=TRIFORCE PIECE=- and you'll be warped to the Overworld again.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   L A Y I N G   D O W N   F L U T E   T R A C K S                   [203-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that we have the Recorder, there's a few things we can get around the
Overworld, namely a couple of Heart Containers. From the entrance to the A
Labyrinth, head south three, east four, north four, east two, and south one to
reach D11. Play the Recorder here and some stairs will magically appear. Head
down and the Old Man will give you the choice between Red Potion and a -=HEART
CONTAINER=-. Will you ever-- JUST GRAB THE HEART CONTAINER.

Now then, we gotta go around our ass to get to our elbow. We're gonna head
back towards the origin by going south one, west one, south two, west two. For
reference, we are at G8, one above the origin. Continue west four, south one,
west two (bottom path), north one, ULDL (up, left, down, left), north three,
east three, north (right stairs), east two, north one (either stairs), east
two, north one up the stairs, and finally west one. Holy balls, was that a
trek.

We're at A7 now, so kill the Lynels (and Peahats if you're patient enough) then
play your Recorder again and another flight of stairs will appear. Head down
and the Old Man will give you the choice of-- Oh, forget it. Every time with
this! You want the Potion? Get the Potion. IF YOU'RE AN IDIOT! Take the -=HEART
CONTAINER=- like a smart person and head back up.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S P E C I A L   D E L I V E R Y                                   [203-4]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There's one more thing we can go ahead and do while we're over here now that
our gear doesn't suck and we have more than three hearts. There will be a lot
of Lynels on this little trek so brace yourself for that. Head east one, south
down the stairs, west five, north up the stairs, west two, south down the
stairs and we're here: B2. Push the leftmost rock either direction to reveal a
staircase. Use the map for help.

            _____________   _______________
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|-|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯   ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯'.|#|
            |    \||            _  |#|   |#|     KEY:
            |/    ||/       _ _|#|  _    |#|
                           |P|L|   |#|   |#|      L  - Letter
               \||          ¯ ¯|#|  ¯    |#|      P  - Push
                ||/             ¯  |#|   |#|      #  - Rock
            ___________________________.'|#|     |-| - Stairs
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
 
Head down the stairs and you'll receive the -=LETTER=- from the Old Man. Now,
we can unlock the Potion Shop. So, let's drop this off really quick. Make sure
you're Recorder is still equipped, face north (or east) and play it. Since
there're no secrets on this screen, it will warp you to the entrance of the E
Labyrinth (if it does not, face north or east and play the Recorder again).
This is Recorder Warping. It will take you to each Labyrinth that you have
completed in Level order. Face north/east to warp forward through the list and
face south/west to warp backward through the list. One important note is that
it will warp you to the locations of the Labyrinths in First Quest, even though
we're in Second Quest (i.e. it will warp you to H5 for A Labyrinth instead of
D5). As far as I have tested, here is where it takes you for each Labyrinth:

   -- E Labyrinth: D8 (same)
   -- A Labyrinth: H5
   -- L Labyrinth: D13 (same)
   -- D Labyrinth: A12 (fairy pond)
   -- Z Labyrinth: E6 (same)
   -- Wizard Hat Labyrinth: C3 (30 rupees here)
   -- Apostrophe Labyrinth: E3
   -- Spiral Labyrinth: G14

Additionally, it will skip any Labyrinths you haven't done. So, from here on
out, I will simply say "warp to such and such" and leave you to it.

Now, from E Labyrinth head east one, south three, and west four to G5. Head
into the cave here and give the Letter to the Old Woman. Now we have unlocked
Potion Shops. Buy a Red Potion and head back out to the Overworld.

Now we have just one more thing to do and that is: buy Monster Bait. For that
we need 60 rupees. So, make sure you have that and hit the Gambling Game if you
don't. To get Bait for that cheap, we have to go back to the Blue Ring shop,
so warp back to E Labyrinth and head east one, north one, east four, north one,
east two, and north one through the hidden stairs. Buy the -=MONSTER BAIT=- for
60 rupees and we're ready to hit the third Labyrinth.

Warp back to the E Labyrinth one more time and head east one, south two, east
five (keep to the top path at F12), north one, west one, and north one up the
stairs. There's a little pond here. The L Labyrinth is hidden just like the
Demon Labyrinth was in First Quest. Play the Recorder to drain the pond and
reveal the entrance then head inside.

   L O V E L Y   L I T T L E   L A B Y R I N T H                     [204-1]

-- G2 - No choice here but to head up to F2.

-- F2 - Kill the six Red Goriyas in here and continue right through the locked
door to the boss. WOW!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   B O M B   D O T   C O M                                   [204-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

That was quick (you'll see why momentarily). For now, our boss here is three
Dodongos. Now, I hope you're genuinely ready for a fight cause... who am I
kidding? It's Dodongos. Let's blow it.
    _______________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: D O D O N G O   \_______________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A giant rhinoceros. It hasn't got so much    | Received:              |
  |  attacking power, but it bounces off attacks   |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  with its thick hide"                          |  -- Triforce Piece 2   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Just like the description says, the Dodongo doesn't have much        |
  |    attacking power, in that it doesn't attack at all.                   |
  |  - He just walks around the room. But this time there's three of them.  |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The Dodongo is impervious to everything in your arsenal except bombs |
  |    but you probably guessed that cause the Labyrinth gave you bombs     |
  |    twice and you were smart enough to figure out the Old Man's clue.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - As the Dodongo walks around the room, lay a bomb in its path. As it  |
  |    walks over the bomb, it will eat it and then the bomb will explode   |
  |    inside it. Do this twice and the Dodongo will perish.                |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If for whatever reason the Dodongo doesn't eat your bomb, the smoke  |
  |    will still stun it and you can run up and slash him to bits during   |
  |    that window.                                                         |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Dodongo is probably the easiest boss in this game. Drop bombs in his   |
  |  path twice or stun him with smoke and hack away with your sword. This  |
  |  is an easy win so dispatch them and I'll see you on the other side.    |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

Well that was easy. So why was this so short? Because, we still have the rest
of the Labyrinth to hit and for some reason they put the boss right at the
front. Grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- that's left behind for you and head back
out to F2.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   U N F I N I S H E D   B U S I N E S S                             [204-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- F2 - Head up now through the other door.

-- E2 - There are six Electric Ropes in here (just normal Ropes but with a
little static charge). Kill them and they will drop bombs for you since you
probably need some after the Dodongo fight. Continue up.

-- D2 - Kill all of the five Blue Goriyas here to open the sealed door above
and then get the map if you didn't grab it already. Continue up.

-- C2 - Kill the six Stalfos in here and grab the -=KEY=- that drops once they
are dead. Continue up. Exciting stuff, right?

-- B2 - There's a Hungry Goriya here, so equip your Monster Bait and feed him
to make him disappear. Continue up through the locked door.

-- A2 - Kill the six Red Goriyas in here and grab the -=MAGIC BOOMERANG=-.
Yippee, or whatever. Head back down five to F2, then right through the Boss
Chamber (the Dodongos will be back but you can just breeze past them, no need
to fight them again) and continue down to F3.

-- F3 - Get the -=COMPASS=- from in here and kill all of the Wall Masters
(there's eight of them). Push the middle stone on the right side to open the
passage.

                 _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 
                |_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|     KEY:
                                  |_|       
                                  |P|>    P - Push Block
                                  |¯|     > - Direction
                |¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|
                 ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯

Head down the stairs kill the Keese down here, then continue up the other side.

-- C1 - Kill the six Red Goriyas here and grab the -=KEY=-. Continue up one.

-- B1 - Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- here and you will be warped back to the
Overworld.

I agree, the order of that Labyrinth is bizarre. It's also a tad dull thanks
to its shape. But now that it's over, we can head to the D Labyrinth. From the
L Labyrinth, head south one, east one, north two, north again up the stairs,
and west two. We're now at B12, the screen that repeats itself. Instead of
heading north four times like we had to in First Quest, our Labyrinth entrance
is on this very screen. Push the far-right stone (up or down) to reveal stairs.
Use the map for help.

-=MAKE SURE YOU HAVE 150 RUPEES BEFORE HEADING IN. IF YOU DON'T, FARM THEM.=-
When you're ready, head on in.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   D   I S   S I L E N T                                     [205-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H2 - Three options here, we're going to go left first.

-- H1 - Use the Blue Candle to light the room. There's three Keese, two Zols,
and three Bubbles in here. Kill the Zols and the Keese and grab the -=KEY=-
that appears. Return to H2 and head up this time.

-- G2 - MINIBOSS - Digdogger. Play your Recorder here to shrink the Digdogger
and beat up the three mini Digdoggers to open the left door. Head through.

-- G1 - We've got two Red Darknuts, two Blue Darknuts, and two Pols Voices in
here. Kill them all (easier said than done) and the -=COMPASS=- will drop for
you. Grab it and head up.

-- F1 - Illuminate the room with the Blue Candle. Now we're going to encounter
some new enemy types in here: Red and Blue Bubbles. There's three Red Bubbles
and one Blue Bubble along with four Darknuts (two of each color). Avoid the Red
Bubbles like the plague (they will disable your sword PERMANENTLY or until you
touch a Blue Bubble). Kill the Darknuts to open the door above. Continue right
through the locked door (you can skip the enemies in here for now, but you'll
have to kill them sooner or later).

-- F2 - MINIBOSS - Aquamentus. Kill the Aquamentus in here by slashing it's
dome and then head through the door on the right.

-- F3 - You've got two Gibdos, two Keese, and two Pols Voices to contend with.
Kill everything and then push far left block in the middle row up to reveal a
staircase in the top right corner.

               _    _    _ _    _    _
              |_|  |_|  |_|_|  |_|  |_|    KEY:
               ^    _    _ _    _    _
              |P|  | |  | | |  | |  | |    P - Push   
               ¯    ¯    ¯ ¯    ¯    ¯     ^ - Direction
              |¯|  |¯|  |¯|¯|  |¯|  |¯|
               ¯    ¯    ¯ ¯    ¯    ¯

Head down the stairs to the basement. Kill the four Keese and grab the -=MAGIC
BOOK=- from the platform on the right. Now we don't have the Magic Wand yet,
but when we do get it, it will immediately be ultra-powerful! Head back up the
stairs and go up through the illusion wall.

-- E3 - Here the Old Man will offer you a Bomb Upgrade. Pay him the 100 rupees
and you'll be able to carry 12 bombs now. Continue left through another
illusion wall.

-- E2 - Killing the five Red Darknuts in here will drop some bombs for you.
Since you just bought the Bomb Upgrade and don't need bombs, feel free to
ignore them entirely and continue left through the locked door.

-- E1 - We've got six Blue Darknuts to deal with. There are two Stone Statues
in the lower corners, but they don't show fireballs, so don't worry about it.
Kill the Blue Darknuts and a Key will drop. Continue up.

-- D1 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill the two Zols in here and head
up again.

-- C1 - Use the Blue Candle to light the room and then kill the five Zols in
here. Grab the bombs that drop if you need and continue right.

-- C2 - Push the block in the middle to the right and continue down.

-- D2 - Two Gibdos, two Keese, and two Pols Voices in here. Kill them all and a
-=KEY=- will drop. Grab it, then bomb the right wall and continue through.

-- D3 - Grab the rupees in here and then head back through D2 and then back up
to C2.

-- C2 - Now push the block up and bomb the right wall. Continue through to C3.

-- C3 - MINIBOSS - Dodongo. Dodge the fireballs from the four Stone Statues
while you kill the Dodongo and then continue up through the next door.

-- B3 - You've got six Blue Darknuts and two Stone Statues in the center. Kill
the Blue Darknuts as quickly as you can and the -=MAP=- will appear.

Fun fact of trivia for you to ponder while you're suffering through prescient
Darknuts and a holy barrage of fireballs: Second Quest was initially planned as
a separate sequel to Legend of Zelda called "Zelda II: Hope You Like Darknuts",
but the title didn't test well with anyone other than masochists, so they made
it into Second Quest instead.

Grab the map you just worked your ass off for and head back down, then left,
then up to B2.

-- B2 - Kill all of the Keese in her and then marvel at the middle finger from
this game as the -=KEY=- appears across the water. Bomb the top wall and head
through.

-- A2 - And here we have our first Thief room. He'll give you the choice
between your life or your money. ALWAYS choose money. ALWAYS. The heart docks
you a FULL HEART CONTAINER PERMANENTLY!! Never choose that. Give the bastard
50 rupees and continue right.

-- A3 - Push the left block in the middle group and a staircase will open in
the top right corner. Head down, kill the four Keese, and continue up the other
stairs to G4.

-- G4 - WATCH OUT FOR RED BUBBLES AS YOU ENTER! Do NOT touch these Bubbles or
you have to backtrack to the one Blue Bubble. Immediately head up through the
locked door to the Boss.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   P R O T O Z O A   P O U N D I N G                                 [205-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now we're gonna fight Digdogger. So, I hope that you've been preparing well for
a fight cause... Digdogger's easy. Far easier than room B3 was. So, let's give
the dog a bone.
    __________________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: D I G D O G G E R  \____________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "Big sea urchins. In spite of their big       | Received:              |
  |  bodies, they shrivel up when attacked. But    |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  watch out! They come on pretty strong."       |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Digdogger doesn't really have any attacks, it just constantly moves  |
  |    around the room. If it touches you, it will do damage.               |
  |  - Also watch out for the four statues in the corner that will be       |
  |    continuously shooting fire at you                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Digdogger's strategy makes him one of the easiest bosses in the      |
  |    game. Make sure you have your Recorder equipped and play it during   |
  |    the fight.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The Recorder melody will cause Digdogger to shrivel up to three tiny |
  |    Digdoggers. Once he's been shrunk down, four slashes with the White  |
  |    Sword will take each one out.                                        |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Digdogger moves pretty fast once it's been shrunk down. You can use  |
  |    the Boomerang to stun it and keep it in place while you whack at it. |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - You'll need to be evading the Stone Statue fireballs the entire      |
  |    time, cause they'll just keep peppering you. They're honestly a      |
  |    bigger threat than Digdogger.                                        |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Digdogger is a giant floating booger and a scaredy-cat. Play your      |
  |  Recorder to shrink it down and then hit it with a Boomerang and hack   |
  |  it to bits. A quick jam session and you'll be outta there in no time.  |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

Once you've slice and diced Digdogger, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- it drops
and head up to the next room, but DON'T GRAB THE TRIFORCE.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Y O U   G O T T A   S N E A K ,   S N E A K                       [205-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Head up through an illusion wall.

-- D4 - Kill the three Red Darknuts in here while avoiding the Stone Statues'
fireballs and the door above will open. Head up.

-- C4 - MINIBOSS - Dodongos. Kill the three Dodongos while avoiding more
fireballs from Stone Statues and the doors will open. Continue up.

-- B4 - There's two Red Darknuts, two Blue Darknuts, and two Pols Voices in
here. Kill them all and then push the fourth block down in the left most column
to the left to reveal a staircase in the top right corner.

                  _   _
                 |_| |_|_ _   _ _ _   S
                 |_| |_|_|_| |_|_|_|_ _     KEY:
                 |_|     |_|     |_|_|_|
                <|P| |¯| |_|     |_|        P - Push
                 |¯|¯|¯| |_|  _  |_|  _     < - Direction
                  ¯ ¯ ¯  |_| |_| |_| |_|    S - Stairs
                   |¯|       |_|     |_|
                    ¯

Head down and kill the four Keese then grab the -=RAFT=- from the platform on
the right. Go back upstairs and head down three to the Triforce room.

-- E4 - Now you may grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- and you will be warped to the
Overworld.

Great, that Labyrinth's over with (and good riddance honestly, that one sucks).
Now we got some rafting around to do. So, from the D Labyrinth entrance, head
west four, south one, east seven, down one, and east one to D16. Step off the
dock to raft north C16. Enter the cave here and the Old Man will give you the
choice between Red Potion or a -=HEART CONTAINER=-. Seriously? We're gonna do
this every time? Just take the damn Heart Container.

Now we can head to the Z Labyrinth. Go back outside and warp to the E Labyrinth
again. Now head east one, south two, and west four to F6. Rafting up from the
dock here will take us to the Z Labyrinth, but there's something we can do to
be more prepared. Head south one then west one and buy a Potion if you need,
then continue north two and head into the cave here. Buy Arrows for 80 rupees
and then return to F6 and raft north. Enter the Z Labyrinth.

   Z   A S   I N   X Y L O P H O N E                                 [206-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H3 - Nothing to do here but head up to the next room.

-- G3 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Illuminate this room with the Blue
Candle and dodge the fireballs from the Stone Statues while you kill the two
Zols in here. Continue left.

-- G2 - Kill the four Like Likes in here to get five rupees, just don't let
them touch you! Continue left.

-- G1 - Light things up with the Blue Candle and kill the three Vires in here
and their Red Keese forms to get the -=MAP=-. Grab it and go back right.

-- G2 - Go down through the locked door.

-- H2 - Don't bother with the four Wizzrobes in here, just avoid the three
Red Bubbles and head left through the illusion wall.

-- H1 - Light the room with the Blue Candle and kill all the Keese for a
-=KEY=- to drop. Grab the Key and head back right.

-- H2 - Head straight right down the stairs to the right. Kill the four Keese
in the basement and ascend the other stairs.

-- A2 - Kill the five Blue Wizzrobes in here and then go to the left side of
the room and push the middle stone in the column inward.

                                     _
                   _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _  |_|
                  |_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_| |_|    KEY:
                  |_|      _ _ _|_| |_|
                  |P|>    |_|_|_|_| |_|    P - Push
                  |¯|               | |    > - Direction
                  |¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|
                   ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯

The door to the right will open so continue through.

-- A3 - We can't fight the Blue Gohma yet, so just continue down.

-- B3 - Evade the Red Bubbles and head down the stairs on the right. Kill the
four Keese down here and collect the -=BOW=- from the platform. Hey, that's
exactly what we need to kill the Gohma. Equip your bow and head back to A3.

-- A3 - MINIBOSS - Blue Gohma. Poke Gohma in the eye a bit and once she's dead,
a -=KEY=- will drop. Grab the Key and head back left, then back down the
stairs.

-- H2 - Immediately beeline back up through the door, ignoring the Wizzrobes
and avoiding the Red Bubbles.

-- G2 - Equip your Blue Candle and head left then up to F1.

-- F1 - Light the room with the Blue Candle. Skip these Wizzrobes, just avoid
the Red Bubbles and go up.

-- E1 - Haul ass to avoid the  cheap shot from the Trap in here and hurry
through the door on the right.

-- E2 - Kill the Zols in here and the -=COMPASS=- will appear. Grab it and head
up through the next door.

-- D2 - There's another key that requires the Stepladder in here. Nothing to
be done about it now, so ignore the Wizzrobes and Like Likes and head through
the door to the right.

-- D3 - MINIBOSS - Manhandla. Bomb the Manhandla to death and it will drop five
rupees for you. Head up through the next door.

-- C3 - There's a tone of Keese in here. Kill them and then go down the stairs.
Kill more Keese in the basement and head up the other flight of stairs.

-- B2 - Kill or ignore the five Vires in here and head through the locked door
on the left to the Boss.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H R E E   H E A D S   A R E   B E T T E R   T H A N   O N E     [206-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Well, it's Gleeok again. And this time he's got three heads, which makes him
tougher, so I hope you're ready for a fight cause... well, it's the same shit
different heads. He's heading for a bruising.
    _____________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G L E E O K   \_________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A huge dragon that has 2 to 4 heads and      | Received:              |
  |  spits out beams at Link. Heads that Link cuts |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  off from its body fly around in the air.      |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - In this specific case we're dealing with a three-head Gleeok. The    |
  |    three heads will shoot fireballs at you.                             |
  |  - Once you separate a head, the head will turn red and fly around the  |
  |    room shooting fireballs at you.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Make sure you've got a decent bit of health going into the fight.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full health, use your sword beams from range to do the   |
  |    bulk of the work.                                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you don't, you'll have to get in close and just trade blows with  |
  |    him. Be consistent with your attacks and Gleeok will die before you  |
  |    do.                                                                  |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - I know that's not much of a strategy but don't blame me, blame the   |
  |    game designers.                                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gleeok is basically just a multi-headed, more annoying version of      |
  |  Aquamentus. Use your sword beams from range if you have full health,   |
  |  otherwise get in close and trade blows with it. You should be coming   |
  |  out the other side in no time.                                         |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

It's a shame he wasn't more headstrong. Once Gleeok bites it, grab the -=HEART
CONTAINER=- and head up to the next room. Grab the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- to warp
back to the Overworld.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A R R O W   T O   T H E   K N E E                                 [206-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've got a quick errand to run before continuing to the Wizard Hat Labyrinth.
And it's one you're gonna really be happy about: Now that we've spelled ZELDA
(and have 12 hearts but more so the ZELDA thing), we can get the Magical Sword!
Unfortunately, since we still don't have the Stepladder, we're going to have to
take a hike to get it.

From the Z Labyrinth entrance: raft south then head south one, west two (get
some Potion if you need), south one, west two (bottom path), north one, ULDL
(up, left, down, left), north three, east three, north one (right stairs), east
two, north one (either stairs), east two, north up the stairs, and then
east two to a screen with rocks in the shape of an arrow. Phew!

Push the fair left rock (tip of the arrow) up or down. Use the map for help.

           "M A S T E R   U S I N G   I T   A N D   Y O U   C A N
                            H A V E   T H I S."

So, take your new blade and enjoy the merge onto easy street. That's all for
our worldly errands, so now we just have to get to the Wizard Hat Labyrinth.
From A11, head west two, south down the stairs, west two, south down the
stairs, and west three to D1. Play the Recorder here and a tombstone will turn

into stairs. Head down to enter the Labyrinth.
