-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   S O R T I N G   I T   O U T                                       [207-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H4 - No other choice but to head up through the next door.

-- G4 - Light this room with the Blue Candle. There's two Yellow Wizzrobes and
three Blue Wizzrobes. Kill them and they'll drop some bombs. Go up.

-- F4 - Ignore everything in here and quickly go left.

-- F3 - Kill the three Vires if you want and continue left through the locked
door.

-- F2 - Ignore everything in here and quickly continue left.

-- F1 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Avoid the Traps in here and push the
far left block up to reveal stairs in the top right corner. Head down and kill
the Keese then grab the -=STEPLADDER=- from the platform. Traversing just got a
whole lot easier. Head back upstairs and go back right two and then down to G3.

-- G3 - Grab the -=KEY=- in here as painlessly as you can and head back up.
Make sure you don't leave with your sword permanently disabled (drink a Potion
if you do).

-- F3 - Head right to F4.

-- F4 - Continue ignoring everything. Bomb the top wall and head through.

-- E4 - Ignore everything in here and continue left.

-- E3 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Get on the island and kill all four
Like Likes in here to get the -=MAP=-. Continue up through an illusion wall.

-- D3 - Ignore everything in here and bomb the right wall. Continue through the
hole. While you're doing that, ponder this interesting tidbit of trivia: when
"Zelda II: Hope You Like Darknuts" tested poorly, they remarketed it as "Zelda
II: Wizzrobe Boogaloo" which was once again a big hit with the masochists and
even got some of the sadist crowd behind it as well. But ultimately not enough,
and we were left with Second Quest once and for all.

-- D4 - Grab the -=COMPASS=- and head back to the left.

-- D3 - While continuing to ignore everything in here, head up now.

-- C3 - Breath a sigh of relieve that it's just six Vires in here. Kill them
all while somehow taking damage and continue right through an illusion wall.

-- C4 - This is a nice little room full of Blue Bubbles. Push the left-most
block in the middle row up to open a stairway in the top right corner. Head
down and kill the Keese as you head up the other stairs.

-- A4 - Kill all of the Keese in here and the bomb the bottom wall. Continue
through.

-- B4 - Grab the -=KEY=- to your left quickly and go back up.

-- A4 - Now continue through the locked door on the right.

-- A5 - MINIBOSS - Gleeok. Just a two-headed Gleeok but we have to kill it. Do
what you do best (or at least adequately) and dispatch it. You'll be rewarded
with five rupees (yay) and the door to the right will open. Continue right.

-- A6 - Have fun with this. Avoid the swarm of Red Bubbles and push the left-
most block up to reveal a staircase. If you have a Potion handy, you can just
take the Red Bubble hit and use your Potion to bring your sword back. Head down
and kill the Keese before continuing up the other side.

-- C6 - Ignore the Manhandla and continue up to the Boss.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   T H E   K R U S T Y   K R A B                                     [207-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once again, we face my favorite boss of the game: Gohma. The lovely crustacean
has gotten all dolled up for us this time in her nicest shade of blue shell.
Now, I really do actually genuinely hope that you're definitely ready for a
fight this time cause... well, she's just as easy as she always ways. Let's
abide by the claw.
    __________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G O H M A  \____________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "The super huge crab that lives in the        | Received:              |
  |  labyrinths. Its hard shell will repulse any   |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  attack. Attack its weak point with a special  |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |  weapon."                                      |                        |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Gohma will run back and forth at the top of her little lair and      |
  |    try to warm you up with some fireballs.                              |
  |  - That's pretty much it.                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Strafe and use your shield to block all of the incoming fireballs.   |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Wait for Gohma to descend from the top and open her eye, then shoot  |
  |    her in the eye with an Arrow. She'll die from one shot.              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you're out of rupees (and thus arrows), you literally can't use   |
  |    anything else, so find some rupees ASAP.                             |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gohma's a crabby bitch that hangs in the back and peppers you with     |
  |  fire. Teach her a lesson by shooting her in the eye with an arrow.     |
  |  You should be able to kill her almost as soon as you walk through the  |
  |  door so she's a quick one.                                             |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

Once she's been sufficiently blinded, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- and head up
through the door. Get the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- to warp out of here.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   O U T   O F   O R D E R                                           [207-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now, we have just one more Heart Container to pick up. So, make your way back
to the origin point (I find it easiest to warp to E Labyrinth and head down),
then go all the way east to H16 and north two to F16. Use the Stepladder to
grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- off the wood platform.

With that out of the way, we're free to head on to the Spiral Labyrinth, which
is actually Level 8, and I do have a reason for this. That reason is that the
Spiral Labyrinth is easier than the Apostrophe Labyrinth, and we'll get the
Magic Wand, Magical Key, AND a Bomb Upgrade that will help us to tackle the
Apostrophe Labyrinth easier. And lastly, it's my guide and you have to do what
I say.

SO, we need to have 100 RUPEES AND MONSTER BAIT for Spiral Labyrinth, so make
sure you have at least 160 (better to max out honestly) and head to the Blue
Ring shop at A15. Buy some -=MONSTER BAIT=- for 60 rupees and then warp back to
E Labyrinth and head east one, north one, west one, north one, and then east
two to B10 (B9 has a Potion Shop if you bomb the north wall -=FOUR TILES=- from
the right, so grab some potion if you need). Use the Stepladder to cross the
river and bomb the north wall -=5 TILES=- from the left. Use the map for help.

           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|

           |#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|
           |#|#|#|#|8|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|#|     KEY:

            _______________________________       #  - Rock

Once you've got Monster Bait, have 100 rupees, and have bombed the wall, head
through the opening to the Spiral Labyrinth.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   G E T T I N G   D I Z Z Y                                         [208-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H8 - Head up through the only door.

-- G8 - Avoid the Red Bubbles (there are a lot) and push the left block up to
open stairs in the top right corner. Head down, kill the Keese, and head up the
other side.

-- B1 - Kill the six Red Goriyas in here and continue to down through the
illusion wall.

-- C1 - MINIBOSS - Dodongos. Ignore the dinosaurs and continue down through the
locked door.

-- D1 - Three Red Bubbles accompany a Blue Bubble around here, which means you
don't need to worry too much about getting bumped. There are four Wall Masters
that you need to kill before you can push the middle block in the right column
over to reveal a staircase.

                 _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 
                |_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|_|     KEY:
                                  |_|       
                                  |P|>    P - Push Block
                                  |¯|     > - Direction
                |¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|¯|
                 ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯

Head down the stairs and kill the Keese before grabbing the -=MAGIC WAND=- from
the platform. Return upstairs and go back up.

-- C1 - Keep ignoring the Dodongos and go right.

-- C2 - There's three Blue Goriyas, three Keese, and two Bubbles in here. Kill
the Goriyas and Keese and bomb the bottom wall. Continue down.

-- D2 - Kill the five Blue Goriyas while avoiding fire from the Stone Statues
and they will drop the -=MAP=-. Pick it up and go back up.

-- C2 - Push the left block in the middle row to reveal a staircase.

               _    _    _ _    _    _
              |_|  |_|  |_|_|  |_|  |_|    KEY:
               ^    _    _ _    _    _
              |P|  | |  | | |  | |  | |    P - Push   
               ¯    ¯    ¯ ¯    ¯    ¯     ^ - Direction
              |¯|  |¯|  |¯|¯|  |¯|  |¯|
               ¯    ¯    ¯ ¯    ¯    ¯

Kill the Keese in the basement and continue up the other side.

-- F8 - Kill the six Electric Ropes in here and continue up.

-- E8 - Kill the Blue Goriyas and head up again.

-- D8 - MINIBOSS - Digdogger. Ignore the Digdogger or kill it and continue up.

-- C8 - Equip your Monster Bait and feed it to the Hungry Goriya here to make
him disappear. Continue up.

-- B8 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Light the room with the Blue Candle
(or Magic Wand). Kill all the Keese in here and they will drop the -=COMPASS=-
for you. Take it and go up.

-- A8 - Kill the five Blue Goriyas in here and they'll drop a -=KEY=-. Get it
and continue left.

-- A7 - Kill the six Blue Goriyas in here to open the doors and continue left.

-- A6 - MINIBOSS - Digdogger. Kill the Digdogger if you want five rupees. Bomb
the left wall and continue through.

-- A5 - Avoid the Red Bubbles in here and kill the four Wall Masters if you
need some bombs. Continue through the locked door on the left.

-- A4 - MINIBOSS - Dodongos. Now we have to actually fight the Dodongos. Kill
them and the door left will open. Continue through it.

-- A3 - Avoid the six Red Bubbles in here (don't worry too much about it, there
will be a Blue Bubble soon) and grab the -=KEY=-. Push the left block in the
middle group to open the stairs. Head down, kill the Keese, and continue up the
other side.

-- E2 - Here's the Blue Bubble if you need it. Head through the locked door on
the left.

-- E1 - Kill the six Stalfos in here and then push the third block from the top
in the left long formation up to reveal stairs in the top right corner.

                    _                 _
                  _|_|    _         _|_|
                 |_|    _|_|      _|_|

                     |P|      _|_|
                   |¯|¯     _|_|    _      P - Push
                 |¯|¯      |_|    _|_|

Head down the stairs and kill the Keese. Grab the -=MAGIC KEY=- from the
platform and return upstairs. Head back to the right and then down.

-- F2 - Push the central block down and go left.

-- F1 - Kill the Electric Ropes in here and go down through an illusion wall.

-- G1 - Kill the three Blue Goriyas and three Keese in here if you want five
rupees, otherwise go right.

-- G2 - Ignore the Keese in here and continue right.

-- G3 - Kill the six Blue Goriyas in here and push the left block up to access
the stairs. Head down, kill the Keese, and go up the other side.

-- E6 - Kill the two Moldorms in here. Bomb the south wall and go through.

-- F6 - There six Goriyas in here (three of each color). Kill them all if you
want five rupees and continue down through the next door.

-- G6 - MINIBOSS - Aquamentus. Kill Aquamentus with three headshots from the
Bow and head through the door to the left.

-- G5 - Kill the four Wall Masters in here while avoiding the Red Bubbles. Push
the middle block in the right column over to open the left door.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   J U R A S S I C   M A L A R K                                     [208-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once again, we face three Dodongos for the final boss. Stone Statues in all
four corners. But get ready for a fight this time cause... nothing. Cause
nothing. They're friggin Dodongos. Let's fossilize these guys.
    _______________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: D O D O N G O   \_______________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A giant rhinoceros. It hasn't got so much    | Received:              |
  |  attacking power, but it bounces off attacks   |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  with its thick hide"                          |  -- Triforce Piece 2   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Just like the description says, the Dodongo doesn't have much        |
  |    attacking power, in that it doesn't attack at all.                   |
  |  - He just walks around the room. But this time there's three of them.  |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - The Dodongo is impervious to everything in your arsenal except bombs |
  |    but you probably guessed that cause the Labyrinth gave you bombs     |
  |    twice and you were smart enough to figure out the Old Man's clue.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - As the Dodongo walks around the room, lay a bomb in its path. As it  |
  |    walks over the bomb, it will eat it and then the bomb will explode   |
  |    inside it. Do this twice and the Dodongo will perish.                |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If for whatever reason the Dodongo doesn't eat your bomb, the smoke  |
  |    will still stun it and you can run up and slash him to bits during   |
  |    that window.                                                         |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Dodongo is probably the easiest boss in this game. Drop bombs in his   |
  |  path twice or stun him with smoke and hack away with your sword. This  |
  |  is an easy win so dispatch them and I'll see you on the other side.    |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

Why they made the absolute easiest boss in the game the boss of the last
Labyrinth is beyond me, but once they're dead, grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- and
head up through the next door. Pick up the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- to be warped out.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   N O T H I N G   T O   S E E   H E R E                             [208-3]

Nothing to do but head to our last Labyrinth. So, from the Spiral Labyrinth,
head west two, south one, east one, south four, and east four to G13. Equip the
Blue Candle and burn the bush where there's just a row of two. Use the map for
help.

-- G2 - Look at the map. Look at it. What the hell shape is that supposed to

-- G1 - Watch out for Traps as soon as you enter! Kill the two Zols in here and
grab the -=COMPASS=-. Head back right to the Entrance and go right.

-- G3 - Nothing to get here, continue right.

-- G4 - Also nothing to get here, continue right avoiding the Red Bubbles.

-- G5 - Kill the three Gibdos, two Red Darknuts, and Blue Darknut here. Push
the third block from the top in the left structure to reveal stairs.

them all and push the left block in the middle group up. Go down the stairs
that appear. Kill the Keese in the basement and grab the -=RED CANDLE=- from
the platform. Go back upstairs and back up to A3 and through the stairs to G5.

-- G5 - Now go through the door on the right.

-- G6 - MINIBOSS - Manhandla. Kill the Manhandla and push the left most stone
up to open the doors. Continue right.

-- G7 - Use the Red Candle to light the room and kill the four Darknuts (two
red/two blue). Continue up.

-- F7 - Kill the Darknuts in here (two red/two blue) and the -=MAP=- will
appear. Grab it and continue up while avoiding Red Bubbles.

-- E7 - Avoid the fireballs from the Stone Statues and kill the five Blue
Darknuts in here. The door above will open and you'll get five rupees to
compensate for the multiple hearts you probably just lost.

-- D7 - Ignore the Darknuts in here and continue up.

-- C7 - MINIBOSS - Blue Gohma. Kill Gohma quickly and continue up.

-- B7 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill the Keese in here and push the
leftmost block up to open the top right stairs. Head down to the basement.
Kill the Keese and continue up the other side.

-- E4 - There's EIGHT Blue Darknuts in here. Say "hell no" to that and head up.

-- D4 - Push the central block up and go right.

-- D5 - Pay the Thief his 50 rupees and go down.

-- E5 - Six Blue Darknuts in here and we have to kill them. Engage in mortal
kombat and once they're dead, push the third block from the top in the left
structure to open the stairs.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   F O R E H E A D                                                   [209-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once again, we face a Gleeok, just with four heads no. I'm curious as to why
Manhandla was never an actual boss in Second Quest, but oh well. Not my chair,
not my problem. Let's not lose our heads here.
    _____________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G L E E O K   \_________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  "A huge dragon that has 2 to 4 heads and      | Received:              |
  |  spits out beams at Link. Heads that Link cuts |  -- Heart Container    |
  |  off from its body fly around in the air.      |  -- Triforce Piece 3   |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - In this specific case we're dealing with a three-head Gleeok. The    |
  |    three heads will shoot fireballs at you.                             |
  |  - Once you separate a head, the head will turn red and fly around the  |
  |    room shooting fireballs at you.                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - Make sure you've got a decent bit of health going into the fight.    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you have full health, use your sword beams from range to do the   |
  |    bulk of the work.                                                    |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - If you don't, you'll have to get in close and just trade blows with  |
  |    him. Be consistent with your attacks and Gleeok will die before you  |
  |    do.                                                                  |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - I know that's not much of a strategy but don't blame me, blame the   |
  |    game designers.                                                      |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |
  |                                                                         |
  |  Gleeok is basically just a multi-headed, more annoying version of      |
  |  Aquamentus. Use your sword beams from range if you have full health,   |
  |  otherwise get in close and trade blows with it. You should be coming   |
  |  out the other side in no time.                                         |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/

And just like that, you triumph again. No number of heads can keep you down.
Grab the -=HEART CONTAINER=- and continue left. Take the -=TRIFORCE PIECE=- to
warp back to the Overworld.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   O F F   T O   M Y   D O O M                                       [209-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And just like that, we've conquered all eight Labyrinths once again. I say "we"
but really you did it, I just typed all these meaningless words. Well the only
thing left from here is to kick Ganon's teeth in once more. Recorder Warp to
C3 and head south down the stairs, east one, north (right stairs), east one,
north up the stairs, west one, north up the stairs, west three to A1. Bomb
the north wall four tiles in on the path to reveal the entrance to Ganon's
Labyrinth. Use the map for help.

There's a Potion Shop at A3 if you bomb the north wall three tiles to the right
of the stairs, so make sure you're stocked up on Potion. When you're ready,
enter the Labyrinth.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   D E A D L I E R   M O U N T A I N                                 [210-1]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- H5 - You may be surprised to see that the Second Quest Death Mountain is
less complicated than in First Quest. Well, don't look a gift horse in the
mouth too long and head up.

-- G5 - All the sealed doors will open since we've completed the eight other
Labyrinths. Head up first.

-- F5 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Kill the two Zols if you want and
head right through the illusion wall.

-- F6 - Ignore the Keese and continue to the right.

-- F7 - Ignore the Wizzrobes (as best you can) and bomb the top wall. Continue
through.

-- E7 - Kill the Patra in here and it will drop the -=MAP=-. Grab it and head
left through the illusion wall.

-- E6 - Kill the two Yellow Wizzrobes and three Blue Wizzrobes in there then
push the only block left to reveal stairs. Head down, kill the Keese, and grab
the -=SILVER ARROWS=-. Head back upstairs and go up through an illusion wall.

-- D6 - Avoid the Red Bubbles and push the left block. Head down the stairs
that open, kill the Keese, and go up the other side.

-- H4 - Ignore the Wizzrobes here and bomb the north wall while avoiding the
Red Bubbles. Continue up.

-- G4 - Kill the two ultrafast Lanmolas to open the sealed doors. They'll leave
you some bombs if you need them. Continue left.

-- G3 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Ignore the Like Likes in here and
continue left.

-- G2 - Ignore the numerous Vires and head up.

-- F2 - Light things up with the Red Candle and kill the Keese in here. Go up
through the locked door.

-- E2 - Push the central block up and bomb the left wall. Continue through.

-- E1 - Immediately go right back to E2.

-- E2 - Push the block to the right now and head up through the door.

-- D2 - Watch out for Traps as you enter! Ignore the Wizzrobes and immediately
head right.

-- D3 - Killing everything in here will get us a Key. But we don't need Keys.
So, ignore all that garbage and bomb the south wall. Continue through.

-- E3 - Kill the five Zols in here and grab the -=COMPASS=-. Return up to the
chaos room.

-- D3 - Ignoring everything still, bomb the top wall and go through.

-- C3 - Ignore the six Blue Wizzrobes here and go through the locked door to
the right.

-- C4 - It's tough but avoid the Wizzrobes and Like Likes in here, especially
the Like Likes, and go up through the door.

-- B4 - The Old Man tells you to go to the next room, so continue left through
the illusion wall.

-- B3 - Avoid the Like Likes in here and continue left.

-- B2 - Ignore the Wizzrobes in here and continue up.

-- A2 - Avoid the Patra and go left through the illusion wall.

-- A1 - Kill the two Lanmolas here and push the left block. Head down the
stairs that open, kill the Keese, and get the -=RED RING=-. Head back upstairs
and go back through the illusion wall to the right.

-- A2 - Now we gotta kill the Patra. Do your worst to it and once its dead,
push the left block and continue down the stairs. Kill the Keese and go up the
other side.

-- B6 - Immediately bomb the right wall before the Wizzrobes kick your ass and
go through.

-- B7 - Take down the Patra in here and the door the right will open. Head
through to fight Ganon!

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   H E R E   W E   G O   A G A I N ,   A G A I N                     [210-2]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

And we're back to fight Ganon again. Guess he didn't have enough of getting
stomped the first time around. That's okay, I like bacon enough for seconds.
    ___________________________
   /  BOSS BATTLE: G A N O N   \___________________________________________
  |------------------------------------------------------------------------\
  |                                                |                        |
  |  ""Link's going to have a difficult time       | Received:              |
  |  trying to destroy Ganon. He's real mean. But  |  -- Princess Zelda     |
  |  even Ganon has his weak point.                |  -- Triforce           |
  |                                                |                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Attacks:                                                               |
  |  - Disappears and shoots unblockable fireballs at you.                  |
  |  - That's it.                                                           |
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Strategy:                                                              |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - You CAN walk on the black parts of this room. The tiles are just for |
  |    decoration. The whole room is solid.                                 |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - While Ganon is fighting like a bitch and being invisible, you gotta  |
  |    find him. Stab blindly around the room until you hit him. He'll      |
  |    appear briefly and then disappear again. Do this four times.         |
  |                                                                         |
  |  - After the fourth hit, Ganon will turn brown-ish and that's your      |
  |    cue. Shoot him with a Silver Arrow and he'll turn to ash.            | 
  |                                                                         |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |                                                                         |
  |  Summary:                                                               |

  |                                                                         |
  |  Ganon's a chump. Whack around blindly with the sword until you hit him |
  |  four times then shoot him with a silver arrow. He's no real threat at  |
  |  all which kinda leaves you wondering how Hyrule ever got into this     |
  |  mess in the first place.                                               |
   \_______________________________________________________________________/
  
That's right. The fight with Ganon is the exact same as in First Quest. Once
you've killed him, grab the Triforce once more from his pile of ashes and head
up through the door.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   A N D   I   F E E L   F I N E                                     [210-3]
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cut down the fires imprisoning Princess Zelda and officially rescue her!

            "T H A N K S   L I N K,   Y O U ' R E   T H E   H E R O
                             O F   H Y R U L E ."

      "F I N A L L Y ,   P E A C E   R E T U R N S   T O   H Y R U L E .
                   T H I S   E N D S   T H E   S T O R Y ."

                        "Y O U   A R E   G R E A T."

             [Y O U R   N A M E   H E R E]    -  [# OF DEATHS]

           "Y O U   H A V E   A N   A M A Z I N G   W I S D O M
                            A N D   P O W E R."

And so concludes The Legend of Zelda. It's been a wild two adventures with you.
I knew you could do it and you proved me right! Congratulations on beating the
first Zelda game. I'll see you right back here for Zelda II: Adventure of Link.

The following maps were made to be used in tandem with this guide. I highly
suggest you print them out or open them in a separate window so that you can
always refer back to them. Every part of this walkthrough will consistently
refer back to the map for ease of navigational directions. You'll notice the
map is a grid made up of different coordinates (i.e. A1, A2, B1, etc.). I will
use these coordinates to describe areas throughout the walkthrough, and that is
in reference to this map! Are you getting that the map is important? It's
pretty much the only way to write a decent walkthrough for this game without
giving you a bunch of lefts, ups, and downs. The map is 8 rows by 16 columns.
The rows are letters and the columns are numbers, hence the coordinate naming
system.

                          L A B Y R I N T H   M A P S
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

                         +---------------------------+
                         |--=         KEY         =--|
                         +---------------------------+
                         |                           |
                         | E - Entrance              |
                         | K - Key                   |
                         | M - Map                   |
                         | C - Compass               |
                         | I - Item                  |
                         | B - Boss Fight            |
                         | T - Triforce Segment      |
                         | Z - Zelda                 |
                         | O - Old Man               |
                         | # - Connected Stairs      |
                         | R - Rupee Room            |
                         | G - Hungry Goriya         |
                         | x - Locked Door           |
                         | + - Barricade Door        |
                         | ! - Bombable Wall         |
                         |                           |
                         +---------------------------+

                       |                               |
                       | E - Entrance                  |
                       | K - Key                       |
                       | M - Map                       |
                       | C - Compass                   |
                       | I - Item                      |
                       | B - Boss Fight                |
                       | b - Mini Boss                 |
                       | T - Triforce Segment          |
                       | O - Old Man                   |
                       | F - Thief                     |
                       | # - Connected Stairs          |
                       | R - Rupee Room                |
                       | G - Hungry Goriya             |
                       | x - Locked Door               |
                       | + - Barricaded Door           |
                       | ! - Bombable Wall             |
                       | ~ - Illusion Wall             |

This section of the guide is devoted to being a completionist for this game.
Since it's an old game, there's not all that much to do with regards to a 100%
playthrough, but there are some things we can touch on so let's do it.


   /\=====================================================================/\
  /__\--------------={  H E A R T   C O N T A I N E R S  }=--------------/__\
 /\  /\                             [HEART]                             /\  /\
/__\/__\===============================================================/__\/__\

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                             F I R S T   Q U E S T
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 01 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, H12
HOW TO GET: Bomb the north wall two tiles to the left of the north path to
reveal a cave. Inside, the Old Man will give you the choice between a Red
Potion or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 02 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, E8
HOW TO GET: Use the Blue Candle to burn the fifth bush from the right to reveal
a staircase. Inside, the Old Man will give you the choice between a Red Potion
or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 03 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, C13
HOW TO GET: Bomb the bottom right corner of the large rock formation in the
middle of the screen to reveal a cave. Inside, the Old Man will give you the
choice between a Red Potion or a Heart Container

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 04 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Eagle Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Aquamentus.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 05 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Moon Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Dodongo.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 06 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Manji Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Manhandla.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 07 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, C16
HOW TO GET: Use the raft to sail north from the dock at D16. Enter the building
there to find the Old Man who will once again give you a choice between a Red
Potion or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 08 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Snake Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Gleeok.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 09 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, F16
HOW TO GET: Use the stepladder to cross the wooden platforms to grab it.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 10 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Lizard Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Digdogger.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 11 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Dragon Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Gohma.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 12 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Demon Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Aquamentus (again).

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 13 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Lion Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Gleeok (again).

                            S E C O N D   Q U E S T

|--= HEART CONTAINER 01 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, C1
HOW TO GET: Push the gravestone in the second column, middle row south to
reveal stairs. Inside, the Old Man will give you the choice between a Red
Potion or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 02 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: E Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Aquamentus.

+--------------------------+

+--------------------------+

WHERE: A Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Gleeok.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 04 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, D11
HOW TO GET: Play the Recorder and a flight of stairs will appear. Inside, the
Old Man will give you the choice between a Red Potion or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 05 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, A7 
HOW TO GET: Play the Recorder and a flight of stairs will appear. Inside, the
Old Man will give you the choice between a Red Potion or a Heart Container.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 06 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: L Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat the three Dodongos.

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 07 =--|

WHERE: D Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat Digdogger

+--------------------------+
|--= HEART CONTAINER 08 =--|
+--------------------------+

WHERE: Overworld, C16
HOW TO GET: Use the raft to sail north from the dock at D16. Enter the building
there to find the Old Man who will once again give you a choice between a Red
Potion or a Heart Container.

|--= HEART CONTAINER 09 =--|

WHERE: Morning Star Labyrinth
HOW TO GET: Defeat the three Dodongos (again).

   /\=====================================================================/\
  /__\-------------={  T H E   P R O   C H A L L E N G E  }=-------------/__\
 /\  /\                             [PROCH]                             /\  /\
/__\/__\===============================================================/__\/__\

So, you've beaten the game and then beaten the Second Quest and then done
everything possible and you still want some more? Well, then the Pro Challenge
just might be for you. The Pro Challenge, also known as the Three Heart
Challenge, is the ultimate test of strength and skill for any Zelda player. If
this seems too hard, I advise you to pass it up and do something more fun. It
is elegantly simple and brutally hard. So, let's dig in.

+------------------+
|--= CONDITIONS =--|
+------------------+

The conditions for the Pro Challenge are as follows:

   Keep the Wooden Sword the entire time.
   Never get a Heart Container.
   Never lose a single life.
   Don't get the Blue or Red Ring.
   Get the Map and Compass in every dungeon.

For an added bonus, you could also choose to not get the Magic Key, which would
force you to actually get keys in Death Mountain, but you don't have to add
that caveat. There are some out there who say the Pro Challenge includes not
using the Wooden Sword. Those people are stupid. It's a Pro Challenge, not an
Impossible Challenge. It's plenty hard enough even with Wooden Sword.

So that doesn't sound too bad to you, eh? Well alright then, let's go over some
tips for completing it.

+-------------------------+
|--= BOSS & ENEMY TIPS =--|
+-------------------------+

Aquamentus: Range is your friend. Arrows/Sword Beams.

Dodongo: Gotta use the bombs, just be careful.

Manhandla: Range. You seeing a trend here?

Gleeok: Practice your Matrix skills and stay at range.

Digdogger: Play that funky Recorder, white boy. And then throw the shit out of
your Boomerang.

Gohma: Normal strategy is the pro strategy: Arrows.

Ganon: Godspeed, my friend. There's no strategy to Ganon other than the normal
strategy. Do your best to stay alive and dodge his fireballs.

Darknut: Bombs.

Wizzrobe: Bombs. Or Blue to Yellow Wizzrobe trick.

Remember: if it isn't 100% necessary to fight something, DON'T fight it. Just
skip it and move on. The Boomerang is really handy since it stuns enemies.

+-------------------+
|--= FIRST QUEST =--|
+-------------------+

Clear Eagle, Moon, and Manji, getting their items. Go to Snake and get the
Stepladder then leave. Go to Lizard and get the Flute then leave. Clear Dragon
and get the Magic Wand. Clear Demon and get the Red Candle. Clear Lion and get
the Magic Book. Now return to Snake and Lizard and clear the bosses. Head to 
Death Mountain and whoop Ganon.

+--------------------+
|--= SECOND QUEST =--|
+--------------------+

Clear E and get the Boomerang. Go to A and get the Recorder then leave. Go to
Wizard's Hat and get the Stepladder then leave. Clear Morning Star and grab the
Magic Wand. Now go back and clear everything else in order: L, D, Z, Wizard's
Hat, Spiral. From there, head to Ganon's Labyrinth and kill the bastard.

+------------------+
|--= IN SUMMARY =--|
+------------------+

Heed my words: this challenge is hard as heck. Seriously don't do it if you
think you will fail; it can be super frustrating. It would be seriously
unfortunate for you to burn yourself out on this great game trying to complete
a silly made-up challenge. The strategies don't change, so you can't really
ask for help. It's just a matter of skill.

If you choose to attempt it: I salute you and good luck. If you choose to
forego it: You're wiser than the rest of us.
